tō raṁjiēṇa tēṇaṁ tēsiṁ chattāṇa sō uvajjhāō । sañcaraṇā parivihiō ṇiciṁtō ciṭui sayaṁ pi ॥ 3 ॥ 46 ॥

jahā ṇarāṇaṁ iha kāmakuṁbhō bhavē sayā kāmiyakajjakārī ।
tahā tavō hōi maṁṇōgayāṇaṁ suhāṇa dāyā khalu tappamāṇō ॥ 27 ॥ 101 ॥
bhāvaṇa suhamaṇakāraya, bhavasāyarataraṇa, duddamakaraṇaturaṁgaha bhāvaṇa kayadamaṇa |
sukkajhāṇauṁppāyaga, kēvalanāṇakara, kāmadhēṇu vara bhāvaṇa ēkka ji hōi para ॥ 28॥102॥
bhāvaṇāē payaṭṭāṇaṁ ummaggaṁ jāi ṇō maṇaṁ । dhammaṭṭhāṇēsu savvēsuṁ suhēsuṁ saṁpayaṭṭaē ॥ 29 ॥ 103 ॥
saṁsārasāyarō ghōrō apārō vi sarīriṇaṁ । bhāvaṇaṁ bhāvayaṁtāṇaṁ gōpayaṁ piva bhāsa ॥ 30 ॥ 104 ॥
duddamā iṁdiyā paṁca hayā ummaggagāmiṇō । bhāvaṇāē dharijaṁti mōkkhamaggē suhāvahē ||31||105॥
bhāvaṇāē suhāē u bhāviyāē ṇiraṁtara । sukkajjhāṇaṁ samārōhē ṇarō kammakkhayaṁkaraṁ ॥ 32॥106॥
bhāvaṇaṁ bhāvayaṁtassa suhāṇuṭuāṇakāriṇō । uppajaē varaṁ nāṇaṁ lōyā'lōyappayāsayaṁ ॥ 33 ॥ 107 ॥
kāmadhēṇū jahā dēi dujjhamāṇī maṇicchiyaṁ । dēvacaṁdēhiṁ sūrīhiṁ vaṇṇiyā bhāvaṇā tahā " ||34|| 108 ॥

" ētthēva jaṁbūdīvammi bhāraha'ddhamma dakkhiṇē । ṇayarīē aōjjhāē āsī āijiṇēsarō ॥1॥ 110॥
avaṁtīvaddhaṇō ṇāma tassuppannō sunaṁdaṇō । tassa ṇāmēṇa saṁjāō avaṁtīṇāma jaṇavaō ॥2॥ 111 ॥
tammi ṇīsēsadēsēsu vikkhāyā ṇāyagā purī । ujjēṇīṇāma paccakkhā dhaṇayassēva ṇaṁ purī ॥ 3 ॥ 112 ॥
jā ya vāvī - taḍāgēhiṁ ujjāṇēhiṁ ya maṁḍiyā । haṭṭa - ppava - sahāīhiṁ ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇē virāiyā ||4 ||113 ॥
paranarālaṁghiyāē u sacchabhāvāē savvayā । mahāsaisaricchāē khāiyāē suvēḍhiyā ॥ 5 ॥ 114 ॥
uttuṁgēṇaṁ suvittēṇaṁ parōvaddavahāriṇā । sajaṇēṇa va suddhēṇaṁ pāyārēṇamalaṁkiyā ॥ 6 ॥ 115 ॥
pālaē taṁ puriṁ rāyā vairisīhō tti ṇāmaō । ṇicaṁ vikkhāyakittīō vērivāraṇakēsarī || 7 ||116॥
tassa'tthi savvabhajjāṇaṁ visiṭṭhā rūvasāliṇī । sōmacaṁda tti nāmēṇaṁ dēvī sōhaggasāliṇī ॥8॥117॥
iō ya atthi tatthēva gōravvō tassa rāiṇō । dhaṇadatta tti ṇāmēṇaṁ sēṭṭhī puṇṇa- guṇālaō ॥9॥118॥
viṇīō uvasaṁtappā dhammiṭṭō sīlasaṁjuō । jiṇiṁda-sāhupāyāṇamārāhaṇasamujjaō ॥10॥119 ॥
sīla - sacca - ṇayōvēyā surūvā cārubhāsiṇī । savvatthōciyakāyavvē rayā atthi subhāriyā ॥11॥ 120 ॥

āgacchissāmi' tō sēṭṭhī jaṁpaē ' mā imaṁ kuṇa । malaō dūradēsammi jēṇa tō ciṭu maṁdirē ' ॥ 54 ॥ 163 ॥

pacchiyāvaggahatthō sō malaē jā pahuttaō । tā dahuṁ māliēṇā'vi puṭṭhō sēṭṭhī savimhayaṁ ॥ 56 ॥ 165 ॥
'sāmi ! kō ēsa bālō ?' tti sēṭṭhī jaṁpai 'mē suō' । harisupphuṇṇa hiyaēṇaṁ māliēṇa phalāṇi tōṁ ॥ 57 ॥ 166 ॥

ahō ! ciṁtābharō majjha jāō aja aṇōvamō" । ēvaṁ ca ciṁtaittāṇaṁ kannayaṁ taṁ visajiuṁ ॥ 80 ॥ 189 ॥
jāi aṁtēurē rāyā ciṁtābhārasamāulō । rāyaṁ ciṁtāulaṁ dahuṁ savvadēvīhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ ॥ 81 ॥190॥
'dēva ! ciṁtāpisāīē ajaṁ ghattha vva dīsaha ' । rāyā payaṁpaī 'dēvī ! saccamēyaṁ na saṁsaō ॥ 82 ॥191॥
vaṭṭaē jōvvaṇē jamhāīmā tēlōkkasuṁdarī' । dēvīhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ 'dēva ! ēsā ēgēva kannagā ॥83॥192॥
aō viōgamēīē na sattā sahiu piya !' । jaṁpiyaṁ patthivēṇā'vi 'kiṁ paryapaha ērisaṁ ? ॥ 84 ॥ 193 ॥

subuddhimaṁtiputtassa, jēṇāgacchai paidiṇaṁ । amhāṇaṁ dēva ! pāsammi, viōgō ṇa vi jāya ' ॥ 86 ॥ 195॥
patthivō vi tayaṁ savvaṁ manniūṇa sahaṁ gaō । hakkārittā mahāmacaṁ subuddhiṁ jaṁpa imaṁ ॥87॥196॥

āimē maṁḍalē rāyā nāṇāvatthē payacchai । bīē ābharaṇaṁ dēi thālāīyaṁ ca sōhaṇaṁ ॥ 162 ॥ 271 ॥

kayāē dēhaciṁtāē vicittaṁ taṁ viyāṇiuṁ । 'kiṁ chuhā bāhaē tujha ? piya ! sāhēhi mē lahum̐' || 174 ॥ 283॥
rahassama kahatēṇaṁ tēṇa ' ēvaṁ ' ti bhāsiē । dāsacēḍī samāiṭṭhā tīē ṇāma piyaṁkarī ॥ 175 ॥ 284 ॥
jahā 'ṇēhi lahuṁ bhaddē ! ammōpāsāō mōyagē' । ' āēsō ' tti bhaṇittāṇaṁ dāsī sigdhaṁ viṇiggayā ॥ 176॥ 285 ॥
dēvīpāsāō ghēttr̥ṇaṁ āgayā sīha kēsarē । vāsagēhassa majjhammi taō bhuttaṁ duvēhiṁ vi ॥ 177॥ 286 ॥
ciṁtiyaṁ āyamaṁtēṇa tēṇa ēvaṁ jahā “ahaṁ । vavaēsēṇa kēṇā'vi jāṇāvēyāmi appayaṁ” ॥178॥287॥
ēvaṁ ciṁtittu jaṁpēi jahā 'acaṁtasuṁdarā । ahō'mī mōyagā kiṁtu ujrēṇīṇīrajōgayā' ॥ 179 ॥ 288 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ rāyadhūyāē hasittā ciṁtiyaṁ maṇē । “kimēyamanyaṁ ēsō jaṁpaē aghaḍatayaṁ ? ॥180॥ 289 ॥
jaō acaṁtadūrammi ujrēṇī summaē purī । tā kahiṁ ajjauttēṇa sā diṭṭā saṁbhavissai ॥ 181 ॥ 290 ॥
"
ahavā vi māigēhaṁ sē nūṇaṁ tattha bhavissai । māyāē ya samaṁ tamhā gamō ēyassa saṁbhavē ॥182॥ 291॥
ēvaṁ ca ciṁtiuṁ tassa dinnō paṁcasugaṁdhiō। taṁbōlō appahatthēṇa mahārāgāirēgaō ॥ 183 ॥ 292 ॥
puṇō vi sanniō tēhiṁ 'niggacchāhi lahu lahuṁ' । tēsiṁ cittaṁ muṇēūṇaṁ bhāṇiyā ṇēṇa sā piyā ॥ 184 ॥293॥
'pāukkhālayakajjēṇa jāmi vaccōgihē ahaṁ । tumē vi pāṇiyaṁ tattha pēsēyavvaṁ khaṇaṁtarē' ॥185॥ 294 ॥
1. bhāsiyā kā0 ॥

ēvaṁ payaṁpiu sigdhaṁ vāsagēhāō niggaō । pucchiṁyaṁ ca 'kahiṁ majjha taṁ turaṁgāi ciṭui ? ' ॥ 186॥ 295॥
bhāṁti tē narā 'ēhi jēṇa daṁsēmu tē tayaṁ' । taō tēhiṁ samēō sō gaō ujjēṇivattaṇiṁ ॥ 187 ॥ 296॥
diṭuṁ ca taṁ tayaṁ savvaṁ cittāṇaṁdakaraṁ paraṁ । jaṁ jaṁ sārayaraṁ kiṁci taṁ taṁ ēkkammi rahavarē ॥ 188 ॥ 297 ॥
saṁgavittāṇa jōēi tē cattāri turaṁgamē । ēgō ya piṭuō baddhō taō tē jaṁpiyā narā ॥ 189 ॥ 298 ॥
'sēsaṁ savvamamañcassa appēyavvamasaṁsayaṁ' । ' ēvaṁ ' tiṁ tēhiṁ saṁlattē taō tē pucchiyā narā ॥ 190॥ 299॥
'gāmaṁgāmēṇa akkhēha maggaṁ ujjēṇigāmiyaṁ । tēhiṁ savvammi akkhāē āruhittā tayaṁ rahaṁ ॥191॥300॥
turaṁgē bāuvēgē tē cōittā gaṁcchaī lahuṁ । pattō ya thōvadivasēhiṁ ujjēṇiṁ taṁ mahāpuriṁ ॥192॥301 ॥

ēvaṁ tu ciṁtiuṁ cittē jaṇaṇī tīē jaṁpiyā । jahā 'mē aṁba ! tāēṇa ēkkasi kuṇa daṁsaṇaṁ' ||234|| 343॥

'bhō ! bhō ! suṇēha mē vakkaṁ tumhē dattāvahāṇayā । aputtassa mahaṁ ēsō puttō dēvēhiṁ āṇiō ॥ 377 ॥ 486॥

'dēva ! uccaṭṭhiyā ēttha kē vi sakkhēttayā gahā । mittaṭṭhāṇaṭṭiyā kē vi tā imaṁ caiva sōhaṇaṁ ॥ 384 ॥ 493॥
laggaṁ ēyammi kajammitā mā kiṁci vilaṁbaha' । ēvaṁ sōūṇa raṇṇā vi āiṭṭhā kiṁkarā ṇarā || 385॥494 ॥

sā āha 'jai na mannēsi mamaṁ tā tujjha niddaya ! । maē mayāē nibrbhataṁ itthīvajjhā bhavissai' ॥ 62 ॥ 592 ॥

iya paḍhama - bitiya - taiyayabhavagahaṇāiṁ samāsaō kahiuṁ । saṁpai cauttha- paṁcamabhavagahaṇāī pavakkhāmi ॥ 1 ॥657 ॥
" atthi ihēva jaṁbuddīvē dīvē bhārahē vāsē paṇuvīsajōyaṇasamuvviddhō paṇṇāsajōyaṇavitthiṇṇō puvvāvarasāgarasamōgāḍhō
bharahakhētta'ddhasīmābhūō vēyaḍḍhō ṇāma pavvaō । jō ya- sarayasamaō vva sapuṁḍarīō, sasisēharō vva saguhō, āhiya- 5
ggibaṁbhaṇagihaṁ va sasihī, baradēvaulaṁ va sasālō, suviyaḍūḍhanaravai bva savijjāharō, juvaisamūhō vva suniyaṁbō tti । kiṁca-
uttuṁgasiharasaṁpriyarayaṇaviṇimmaviyajiṇaharā''vāsō । āvāsiyavijjāharanayaravirāyaṁtasēḍhijuō ॥1॥658 ॥
'juyalaṭṭhiyasura - kinnara - siddha- samāraddhasuddhagaṁdhavyō । gaṁdhavvakāmiṇīyaṇamucchāvijtavīṇasarō ॥2॥659 ॥
sarasahariyaṁdaṇahumasugaṁdhapūraṁtasayaladisivivarō । varasyaṇaṇiyaṁracēṁcaiyasiharasayasaṁkulō rammō ॥3॥660॥
tattha ya dakkhiṇāē sēṭīē asthi rahanēuracakkavālaṁ ṇāma ṇayaraṁ । jaṁ ca duhā vi sasālaṁ, duhā vi sapariha, duhā
visasaraṇaṁ, duhā vi saramaṇīyaṁ, duhā vi sarāyaṁ, duhā vi saṁppaṇṇaṁ ti । avi ya-
1. juvala pā0 vinā ॥। 2. 'yaraciṁca' jē0 kā0 ॥। 3. sapattaṁ ti pā0 ||

dariyāriharikisōrayadappasamuddalaṇatikkhaṇahasarahō । ṇīsēsapayāpālaṇabharayasamuddharaṇadhōrēō ॥ 6 ॥ 663 ॥

vi susavaṇā, duhā vi sudarisaṇā, duhā vi sukaṁpriya, tti । avi ya-

kāyavyō । āsaggīvō vi cittē avadhāriūṇa ḍiō saṁbhāvatthō । iō ya āsaggīvēṇa aṇāgayamēva sīhavā-
vāyaṇaparikkhāṇimittaṁ tattha ṭhāṇē kōḍubiyā sāliṁ rōpāviyā । tē ya sīhāō sāmaṁtēhiṁ vāraṁvārēṇa rakkhāviyā । taō
tammi samaē puṇō vi pēsiō annō dūō, jahā - ' avāraē vi saṁpayaṁ tumbhēhiṁ sālī rakkhēyavvō' । taō payāvaiṇā
kumārē aṁbāḍēūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ, jahā - 'tumha duvvilasiyaphalamēyaṁ, jaṁ akālamaccū khavaliō, jaō avāraē cēva duṭṭhā'' ēsō
ēsa samāgaō' tti । taō bhaṇiyaṁ kumārēhiṁ - 'tāya ! vīsatthā ciṭṭhaha tumbhē, amhē sālirakkhaṇatthaṁ gacchāmō' ।
rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ - 'putta ! bālā tubbhē, tā acchaha gihē cēva, ahaṁ sayamēva gamissāmi' । taō dō vi kumārayā nicchayaṁ
kāūṇa vāraṁtassā'vi rāiṇō sabala - vāhaṇā gayā tattha jattha sālī rakkhijai, pucchiyā ya karisayā, jahā - 'kahaṁ
puvvillēhiṁ sālī rakkhiō ? ' । tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ - 'cāuraṁgabalēṇaṁ saṇṇaddhabaddhakavaēhiṁ ' । tiviṭṭuṇā bhaṇiyaṁ - 'jai ēvaṁ tō

' vaddhāvijasi naravara ! juvaraṇṇō akkakittiṇō bhajjā । ṇāmēṇa jōimālā sūrasamaṁ pasaviyā puttaṁ ' ॥40॥722 ॥

ca jāva parivaḍūḍhaē kumārō tāva samāgayā abhiṇadaṇa - jagaṇaṁdaṇābhihāṇā cāraṇasamaṇā । tēsiṁ ca samīvē dhammamā-
yanniūṇa akkakittissa rajjaṁ dāūṇa pavvaiō jalaṇajaḍī । akkakittī vi pālaē vijjāharāhivattaṁ ।
ētthaṁtarammi ya sō saccabhāmājīvō sōhammāō caviūṇa uppannō jōimālāganbhē dhūyattāē, diṭṭhā ya aṇāē sumiṇaē

ēyammi ya samayammi sasabiṁduṇā ṇēmittiēṇa kahiyaṁ sayaṁpabhādēvīē vijayabhaddakumāra pahāṇapariyaṇasamanniyāē, jahā -
'accaṁta bhīsaṇā uppāyā raṇṇō tivvaṁ bhayaṁ ṇivēyaṁti, tā gavēsaha kahiṁci sigdhaṁ, jaō rāyā sirivijaō saṁpayaṁ
jīviyasaṁsaē baṭṭai' । ētthaṁtarē paumiṇikhēḍasāmī saṁḍillāyaṇaṇēmittiō mahārahavarārūḍhō 'na bhēyavvaṁ na bhēyavvaṁ' ti

kusalaṁ, nitthiṇṇā ya mahaī āvayā, paraṁ kiṁci māṇasaṁ dukkhamāsi, taṁ pi muhuttaṁtarēṇa avagacchissai' ।
1

ēvaṁ ca tāṇa dōṇha vi jujjhatāṇaṁ balāṇa aṇavarayaṁ । sāhāviyajujjhēṇaṁ vijjāhiṁ vigappiēṇaṁ ca ॥ 75 ॥ 915 ॥
samaikkatō māsō thōvūṇō jāva tāva jujjhammi । nivaasaṇighōsa kumarā bhaggā parasēnnapaharahayā ॥ 76 ॥ 916॥
tē bhaggē nāūṇaṁ samuḍiō asaṇighōsanaranāhō । hakkaṁtō vaggatō rē ! rē ! rē ! ṭhāha mamahutaṁ ॥77॥917॥
ṇāsēmi jēṇa dappaṁ khaṇēṇa tumhāṇa ēttha, kiṁ bahuṇā ? ' । iya jaṁpiyammi kumarā abbhiṭṭā tassa ṇaravaiṇō ॥78॥918 ॥
tō tēṇa dappiēṇaṁ vijābalasaṁjuēṇa hammaṁtā । tē amiyatēya kumarā abhaggacittā vihu ṇiyattā ॥79॥919॥
tē bhajaṁtē daḍuṁ sirivijayaṇarāhivō sadappiṭṭō । uṭṭhēi asaṇighōsassa sammuhaṁ rōsataṁba'cchō ॥80॥ 920॥
bhaṇai ya 'rē ! rē ! pāviṭu ! duṭṭu ! ṇillajja ! dhiṭu ! kāurisa ! । maṁ vaṁciya maha dēviṁ haramāṇō kiṁ na yāṇāsi ? ॥ 81 ॥921 ॥
tā jai si suhaḍavāyaṁ uvvahasi valāhi tō mamāhuttaṁ । jēṇa samāṇēmi lahu kalattavēraṁ imaṁ aja' ॥82॥922 ॥
taṁ suṇiya asaṇighōsō jaṁpai 'bhō ! sāhu sāhu sāhu tti । jai jaṁpiyaṁ karissasi tō hōsi dhuvaṁ tumaṁ suhaḍō' ॥83॥ 923॥
iya jaṁpiūṇa ēsō sirivijayaṇarāhivassa abbhiṭṭō । jujjhati dō vi suhaḍā āraṇṇayamattahatthi vva ॥84॥924॥
baggati dō vi, gati dō vi, paharaṁti dō vi āruṭṭā । vaṁcaṁti dō vi paharē sura-siddhagaṇēhiṁ dīsaṁtā ॥ 85 ॥ 925 ॥

aha rusiuṁ sirivijaō khaggēṇāhaṇiya kuṇai dōkhaṁḍaṁ । jā asaṇighōsarāyaṁ tā jāyā dōnni tē sahasā ॥86॥926 ॥
jā tē vi hu rōsēṇaṁ dō khaṁḍai tāva tē vi cattāri । jāyā'saṇighōsaṇivā tā tē vi duhaṁḍaē ēsō ॥87॥ 927 ॥
jāyase asaṇighōsā, ēvaṁ baddhaṁti khaṁḍiyā saṁtā । kiṁ bahuṇā ? jāyāiṁ sayāṇi ṇivaasaṇighōsāṇaṁ ॥ 88 ॥ 928 ॥
tō sirivijaō rāyā parisaṁtō suṭu tāṇi khaṁḍaṁtō। ētthaṁtarammi siddhā bijjā siriamiyatēyassa ॥89॥29॥
pattō ya jhatti ēsō ahiḍiō tīē pavaravijjāē । samaraṁgaṇammi tō taṁ daddr̥ṇaṁ asaṇighōsabalaṁ ॥90॥ 930 ॥
kēsarikisōrayassa va naṭuṁ sahasa tti mayagalakulaṁ va । taṁ nāsaṁtaṁ dahuṁ mahajālaṁ bhaṇai ēsō vi ॥91॥931॥
'jaha na vi nāsai ēyaṁ taha kāyavvaṁ duyaṁ taē aṁba !' । tō tīē mōhiyaṁ taṁ miyatēyaṁ saraṇamallīṇaṁ ॥ 92 ॥ 932 ॥
rāyā vi asaṇighōsō'miyatēyaṁ āgayaṁ niēūṇa । jā ṇaṭṭō tā bhaṇiyā vijjā vijjāmuhī tēṇa ॥ 93 ॥933॥
'dūrāō vi hu ēsō āṇēyavvō taē mahāpāvō' । ' ēvaṁ 'ti hōu vijjā pahāviyā tassa paṭṭī || 94 ॥ 934॥
sō tīē parabbhaṁtō saraṇaḍāṇaṁ kahiṁci alahaṁtō । ōyarai dāhiṇa'ḍūḍhē bhārahakhēttassa majjhami ॥ 95 ॥ 935 ॥
tattha vi sīmanagavarō atthi samuttuṁgasiharēciṁcaiō । varaṇayaraṁ va susālō, puhaīṇāhō vva varakaḍaō ॥ 96 ॥ 936 ॥

tuha sāmittaṇasaṁgēṇa sāmi ! sunnēṇa'sārasaṁsārē । saṁsariyaṁ sasarīrayasattusamūhē samatthammi ||4||954 ॥
tuha jhāṇā vimuhēṇaṁ mōhamahārāyavasagaēṇa maē । pattāiṁ dukkhāiṁ nāraya - tiri - maṇuya - dēvēsu ॥5॥955॥
chiṁda-bhiṁdaṇamāī dukkhaṁ rayaṇāiṇarayapuḍhavīsu । jaṁ pattaṁ taṁ muṇiuṁ jāyai ukkaṁpaō majjha ॥ 6 ॥ 956 ॥
tikkhaṁ kakkhaḍadukkhaṁ kharakhiimāī - tirikkhalakkhēsu । khinnēṇa'kkhaliyaṁ ṇāha ! khēviyaṁ jaṁ aṇakkhēyaṁ ॥ 7 ॥957॥
gururōya-sōyagaṁgātaraṁgapariragaṁṇē gayarāga ! । gamiyaṁ maē agaṇiyaṁ guviladuhaṁ naragaigaēṇaṁ ॥ 8 ॥ 958 ॥
suravisarēsu vi īsā -visāyamāī duhaṁ maē sahiyaṁ । ii tuha virahē bhayavaṁ ! bhavabhramaṇaṁ jaṁ tayaṁ juttaṁ ॥ 9॥ 959॥
iṇhi puṇa jiṇapuṁgava ! pattē vi tumammi sāmiē pavarē । jaṁ mōharāyasēnaṁ bāhai acchērayaṁ taṁ mē ॥ 10॥ 960॥
vārijaṁtō vi jaō ēsō kavaēṇa baṁbhamaiēṇa । maṁ rāō gaṇiaṁbagamaggaṇaṇigarēṇa vigalēi ॥ 11 ॥961 ॥
dōsō vi dariyacōrō tuha samayabalēṇa dhariyapasarō vi । avaharai mamāhiṁtō jiṇavara ! hā pasamavararayaṇaṁ ॥ 12 ॥962॥
kōvō davaggisarisō tuha vayaṇajalēṇa sicyamāṇō vi । jaṁ tāvēi maha taṇuṁ taṁ mannē garuyamacchariyaṁ ||13|| 963॥

māi tti vaṁsajālīsarisā tuha vayaṇaparasuṇā ṇāha ! । mūlāō vi chijaṁtī jaṁ baḍūḍhai vimhaō taṁ mē ||15|| 965॥

ahiṇaṁdiyāē puttā dō ṇāmaṁ iṁdu - biṁdusēṇa tti । tattō ya dharaṇijaḍhamāhaṇassa dāsō tahiṁ pattō ॥ 2 ॥ 979 ॥

ahiṇaṁdiya sirivijaō, jōippaha sīhaṇaṁdiyā cavi ṁ । saccabhāmā vi imā jāyā dēvī sutāra tti ॥ 7 ॥ 984 ॥
kavilō vi tīē virahē aṇuhavaī dāruṇaṁ mahādukkhaṁ । kēttiyamēttē vi diṇē gamēi sō aṭṭajhāṇēṇa ॥8॥ 985 ॥
annamma dinē mariuṁ bhamiō sō vivihatiriyajāīsu । aṇuhavamāṇō dukkhaṁ aṭṭajjhāṇassa dōsēṇaṁ ॥ 9 ॥ 986 ॥
khōḍittu tahiṁ kammaṁ bahutarayamakāmaṇiñjarāē u । bhūyarayaṇāḍavīē ērāvaisariyatīrammi ॥ 10 ॥ 987 ॥
asthi bahuviḍavisaṁkulaphala - phullasamāulaṁ mahārammaṁ । āsamapayaṁ visālaṁ bahutāvasajaṇiyaāvāsaṁ ॥ 11 ॥ 988 ॥
tattha'tthi jaḍilakōsiyanāmō varatāvasō suguṇakaliō । tassa'tthi pavaṇavēgā nāmēṇa tāvasī bhajjā ॥ 12 ॥ 989 ॥
tī kucchisi taō uppannō kavilasaṁtiō jīvō । mōttūṇa tiriyajāiṁ akāmaō khaviyabahukammō ॥ 13 ॥ 990 ॥

jāō ya ṇiyayasamaē pasūikammammi tassa vihiyammi । bārasamadiṇē vittē uviyaṁ sē dhammilō ṇāmaṁ ॥ 14 ॥ 991 ॥
aha kamasō vaḍhatō tāvasa kumarattaṇammi saṁpattō । gēṇhai ṇiyapiudikkhaṁ pālēi tahiṁ niyaṁ kiriyaṁ ॥ 15 ॥ 992 ॥

pavaravimāṇārūḍhaṁ suravarariddhiṁ viḍaṁbayaṁtaṁ va । taṁ daduṇaṁ ciṁtai " ahamavi jai ēva vaccāmi ॥ 17 ॥ 994 ॥
tā jai imassa phalamatthi kiṁci kaṭussa tavavisēsassa । tō ahamavi ēvaṁ ciya hiṁḍējjā annajammammi " ||18|| 995 ॥
ēvaṁ ca kayaṇiyāṇō mariuṁ vēyaḍḍhaṇagavarē rammē । sēḍhīē uttarāē nayarīē camaracaṁcāē ॥19॥996॥

piyarēhiṁ asaṇighōsō tti ṇāma vihiyaṁ suyasya ṇiyayassa । sō ya tumaṁ bhō ṇaravara ! jō pucchasi majjha pāsatthō ॥ 22 ॥999॥ 10

ēvaṁ niyapuvyabhavē sōūṇaṁ amiyatēya - sirivijayā । asaṇighōsa sutārā sahasa ciya vimhayaṁ pattā ||25||1002 ॥
ēvaṁ ca kēvaliṇā parūviē samāyanniūṇa ṇiya- ṇiyapuvvabhavē acaṁtaṁ vimhiyāṇi amiyatēya-sirivijayā-
Ssaṇighōsa sutārāṇāmāṇi cattāri vi jaṇāṇi, paramasaṁvēgā''vannāṇi ya । taō pucchiō bhayavaṁ kēvalī
amiyatēyavijjāharāhivēṇaṁ, jahā- 'bhagavaṁ ! kimahaṁ bhaviō, abhaviō ?' tti । taō pakkhubhiyakhīrasa-
muddasaddāṇukāriṇā gaṁbhīra-dhīrasarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ayala kēvaliṇā - bhō amiyatēyamahārāya ! mā aṇivvuōṁ hōhi, jamhā iō
ṇavamē bhavē iha cēva bharahavāsē hōhisi tumaṁ kirīḍabaddhaṇaraṇāhasahassabattīsagapaṇayapāyapaṁkaō cōddasamahārayaṇasāmī
rṇavamahāṇihāṇabasasaṁparjjatasayalasamīhiō tisamuddamēhalāpatapuhaiṇāhō paṁcamō cakkavaṭṭi, tti । tahā tammi cēva jammē
paṇamaṁtasayalākhaṁḍalamaṁḍalamauliviyaliyapāriyāyabahalamālāmiliyacalaṇakamalajuyalō sōlasamō saṁtiṇāhaṇāmō titthayarō
tti, sirivijaō ya tuha paḍhamaputtō paḍhamagaṇaharō bhavissai' । taṁ ca ṇisāmiūṇa bahalarōmaṁcakaṁcuitamuttīhiṁ puṇō
vinnattaṁ, pucchiyaṁ ca amiyatēya - sirivijaēhiṁ, jahā- 'bhayavaṁ! kāṇi gihavāsaṁ pālayaṁtāṇaṁ uciyāṇi vayāṇi bhavaṁti ?
bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ - 'paṁca aṇubvayāṇi, tiṇṇi guṇavyayāṇi cattāri sikkhāvayāṇi' । taō dōhiṁ vi jaṇēhiṁ gahiyāṇi
gihatthōciyāṇi vayāṇi । asaṇighōsēṇa vi ṇiyajēṭuputtō assaghōsaṇāmō pakkhittō amiyatēyassa ucchaṁgē, bhaṇiyaṁ
ca - 'ēyassa annēsiṁ ca maha suyāṇaṁ bhalējjāsi,' tti bhaṇatō aṇēyarāyasamanniō kāūṇa bhayavaō tipayāhiṇaṁ vinnaṁ-
viumādattō । avi ya-

tē āvaṁtē dahuṁ jhaḍatti abbhuḍiō amiyatēō । vaṁdaṁti tē vi muṇiṇō paḍimāō jiṇidacaṁdāṇaṁ ||11|| 1020॥

"naravara ! suṇēhi vayaṇaṁ, jaha bhaṇiyaṁ jiṇavarēhiṁ samayammi । jīvō aṇāiṇihaṇō aṇāikammēhiṁ saṁjuttō ॥ 1 ॥ 1023 ॥

tā ṇaravara ! apamāō kāyavyō ṇiccamēva dhammammi । jamhā hu āgamadharā bhaṇati ēyārisaṁ vayaṇaṁ ॥ 3 ॥ 1025 ॥
“pūyā jiṇidēsu, raī vaēsu, jattō ya sāmāiya-pōsahēsu । dāṇaṁ supattē, savaṇaṁ sutitthē, susāhusēvā sivalōyamaggō” ॥4॥1026॥
paidiyahaṁ ciya ēyaṁ kāyavvaṁ, aṁtaraṁ ṇa kāyavvaṁ । jamhā hu aṁtarēṇa maṇasā vi ēṇa pāvē ||5||1027 ॥
dukhāī aṁtarālē, puṇō vi sō kkhāī aṁtarālammi। jaha dhaṇaō sēṭṭhisuō macchōyarabīyakayaṇāmō" ॥6॥1028 ॥

kaiyāviṇa mē jittaṁ tā saṁpai dēhi kiṁci mē davvaṁ । aha ṇa vi tō ajēva ya ṇa hōsi taṁ majjha hatthāō' ॥ 22 ॥1054 ॥

“jaṁ kira vihiṇā lihiyaṁ taṁ ciya pariṇamai, kiṁ viyappēṇa ? । iya bhāviūṇa dhīrā vihurē viṇa kāyarā hōṁti” ॥ 33 ॥ 1065 ॥
taṁ pēcchiūṇa dhaṇaō hiyaē ciṁtēi suṭu tuṭumaṇō । “ laddhā ahō ! samagghā ēsā gāhulliyā ajja || 34 ॥ 1066॥
savvassaṁ pi hu dijau jai kaha vi tahā vi pāvaē nēya । ēīē phuḍaṁ mōllaṁ ahō ! salāhā imā saṭṭī ” ॥ 35॥ 1067॥
ētthaṁtarammi pattō jaṇaō pucchai ya 'putta ! kiṁ kiṁci । vavahariyaṁ aja taē, uyāhu nō ?' bhāṇiē ēvaṁ ॥ 36 ॥ 1068॥
pāsaṭṭiēhiṁ laviyaṁ 'vavahariyaṁ aja tujjha puttēṇa । gahiyā ēkkā gāhā dīṇārāṇaṁ sahassēṇaṁ' ||37||1069॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ sēṭṭhī jaṁpai kōvēṇa phuriyaaharōḍō । 'khāhisi ērisaēṇaṁ vēbahārēṇaṁ ṇa saṁdēhō ||38||1070 ॥
tā uṭusu ēyāō ṭhāṇāō, uvavisāhi annattha । jēṇa sayaṁ cēva ahaṁ karēmi kaya - vikkayaṁ kiṁci' ॥ 39॥1071॥
iya bhaṇiō ēsō vi hu viṇiggaō uṭṭhiūṇa haṭṭāō । “jaṁ kiṁra vihiṇā lihiyaṁ iccāi " maṇēṇa ciṁtatō ॥40॥1072॥
ṇiggacchai ṇayarāu vi aḍavīē sammuhaṁ aha payaṭṭō । paccāsannammi ya puravarassa aha uttaradisāē ॥ 41 ॥ 1073 ॥
jaṁ ciṭuē araṇṇaṁ saṁpattō tattha diṇa'vasāṇammi । pēcchai ya tappa sē mahāmahaṁta saraṁ ēkkaṁ ॥ 42 ॥ 1074॥ avi ya-
tuṁga - vitthiṣṇapālīē saṁsōhiyaṁ, maccha-jalahatthi - magarāisaṁkhōhiyaṁ ।
sarasaphalaṇamiyataruṇivahasuvicittayaṁ, viyaḍasōvāṇapaṁtīhi suvibhattayaṁ ॥ 43 ॥ 1075 ॥
1. vavasāēṇaṁ pā0 | 2. kiri jē0 ॥

suyaṇacittaṁ va aigahira sacchāsayaṁ, aḍūḍhagēhaṁ va varalacci āvāsayaṁ ।
aḍavimajjhaṁ va kamalōhaparirammayaṁ jaiṇasamayaṁ va acaṁtabahusāvayaṁ ॥ 44 ॥ 1076 ॥
cakkavāēhiṁ ṇivamaggamiva caḍḍiyaṁ, rāyahaṁsēhiṁ ṇivagēhamiva maṁḍiyaṁ ।
bhuyagavayaṇaṁ va acaṁtasuvisālayaṁ, kāṇaṇā-''bhōgaṭhāṇaṁ va sumahālayaṁ ॥ 45 ॥ 1077॥ ti ।
taṁ ērisayaṁ jalāsayaṁ pahiyajaṇāṇa pivāsaṇāsayaṁ । daṭṭu kuṇai sumajaṇaṁ dhaṇaō bahusama - dāhamajaṇaṁ ॥ 46 ॥1078 ॥
uttariūṇaṁ ca taō bahaladalāvariyadīhasāhālaṁ । vaḍapāyavamallīṇō raēi paṇṇūrasattharayaṁ ॥47॥1079॥
sumarittā guru- dēvē puṇō vi āvattiūṇa taṁ gāhaṁ । suttō khaṇaṁtarēṇaṁ jā ciṭui jaggirō tāva ॥48॥1080 ॥
daḍha kaṭhiṇadīhabāhō acaṁtuvyaddhapiṁḍiyājuyalō । masiṇiyarasarisavaṇṇō saradhaṇuṁ varavāvaḍakaraggō ॥49॥1081॥
hariṇāighāyaṇaraō vāhajuvāṇō tahiṁ samaṇupattō । rayaṇīpāraddhikaē bahaladumāvariyataṇubhāō ॥50॥1082 ॥
āyaḍriḍhaya kōyaṁḍō jalapāṇatthaṁ samāgaē sattē । jā jōyaṁtō acchai dhaṇaō uvvattaē tāva ॥ 51 ॥1083 ॥
taṁ sukkapattasaddaṁ sōuṁ vāhēṇa tassa saddassa । mukkō āyannasarō pāē viddhō imō tēṇa ॥52॥1084॥
nāō ya luddhaṇaṁ viddhō ēsō ti ṇiyayalakkhēṇa । jā jāi tassa pāsē tā paḍhai imō vi taṁ gāhaṁ ॥ 53 ॥ 1085 ॥

3
<pb n="132"/>

sōūṇa tayaṁ vāhō ciṁtai " hā hā ! kayaṁ akajaṁ ti । jaṁ ēsa kōvi pahiō viddhō bāṇēṇa ēttha ḍiō" ॥54॥1086 ॥
pabhaṇai ya 'kattha suṁdara ! viddhō aṁgē ayāṇamāṇēṇaṁ ? | majjha khamējasu iṇhi' iya bhaṇiuṁ kaḍūḍhaē bāṇaṁ ॥ 55 ॥। 1087 ॥
jāva vaṇapaṭṭabaṁdha karēi tā vāriō imēṇa imō । 'mā baṁdhasu vaṇapaṭṭaṁ ruhiraṁ ṇikkalau tāka imaṁ ॥ 56 ॥ 1088 ॥
ahamēva paṭṭayaṁ pi hu baṁdhissaṁ, vacca taṁ ṇiyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ' । iya bhaṇiō sō vāhō jāi taō yiyāṇammi ॥57॥1089 ॥
ēsō vi bhavasarūvaṁ bhāvēṁtō jāva ciṭuē tattha । tā lōhiyagaṁdhēṇaṁ bhāruṁḍā pakkhiṇō pattā ॥ 58 ॥1090 ॥
tēhiṁ vi 'maēllaō' tti ya kāūṇuppāḍiō sacaṁcūē । ṇīō samuddamajjhē mukkō dīvammi aḍavīē ॥59॥1091॥
'khāmi' tti jā ṇirikkhaṛa tā jīvaṁtaṁ tayaṁ ṇiēūṇa | mēllai dayāpariṇaō uḍḍittā jāi annattha || 60|| 1092॥
dhaṇaō vihu uḍittā jāva palōēi savvadisibhāē । tā pēcchai taṁ aḍaviṁ bhayajaṇaṇaṁ taruvarāiṇṇaṁ ॥ 61 ॥ 1093 ॥ avi ya-
jā yē sabhīmā ajjuṇajuyā ya siripaṁḍavāṇa sēṇa vva । sarasayaṇiciyā khaggāulā ya saṁgāmabhūmi vva ॥62॥1094॥
mattagaiṁdasaṇāhā paumāsaṇasōhiyā ya lacchi bva । nisiyarapiya vva davamasimailā sivarāva bhīmā ya ॥ 63 ॥ 1095 ॥
jiṇaāṇa vva mahāvayadurasaṁcārā susāvayajuyā ya । mahaṇayari vva susālā dīviyasayasaṁkulā cēva ॥ 64॥1096॥
1. ya subhī0 jē0 kā0 ॥

"
mayasayajuttā jaliyāṇalā ya jā sā masāṇabhūmi vva । laṁka vva pavayabhajirasālā sapalāsayā yatti ॥ 65 ॥ 1097॥
taṁ ērisiṁ ṇiē ṁ acaṁtaṁ bhīsaṇaṁ mahāaḍaviṁ । ciṁtai dhaṇaō " hā ! kaha kajjamiṇaṁ pariṇayaṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 66 ॥1098 ॥
jaṁ kira vihiṇā lihiyaṁ iccāī jīva ! ciṁtasu maṇammi । jēṇa'jja imaṁ savvaṁ aṇuhavasiddhaṁ tuhaṁ jāyaṁ ॥67॥1099 ।।
ēvaṁ paribhāvēuṁ jā hiṁḍai tattha raṇṇamajjhammi । tā pēcchai jalahitaḍaṁ apāraṇīrāulaṁ bhīmaṁ ॥ 68 ॥ 1100॥
abbhutaṁ pivē tuṁganīra kallōlataṇuvihāēṇa । āliṁgaṁtaṁ piva gurutaraṁgabāhāhiṁ pahiyajaṇaṁ ॥ 69॥1101 ॥
agghaṁtaṁ piva vēlucchalaṁtasumahaggharayaṇaṇiyarēṇa । hakkāraṁtaṁ piva vivihavihagasaddēhiṁ aṇavarayaṁ ॥ 70 ॥ 1102 ॥
ābhāsaṁtaṁ piva khubbhamāṇajalajalayarāṇa rāvēṇa । taṁ daṭṭu chuha-taṇhāhiṁ pīḍiō jōyai phalāī ॥ 71 ॥ 1103 ॥
pēcchai ya ēgadēsē kiṁci puraṁ uvvasaṁ saḍiya - paḍiyaṁ । khaḍahaḍiyadēva maṁdirakiṁcīdaradiṭṭhagambhaharaṁ ॥ 72॥1104॥
vaṇamahisatikkhasiṁga'ggaghāyasaṁbhaggavalahiyāvayavaṁ । vaṇakarivisāṇapēllaṇaṇivaḍaṁta kavāḍasaṁpuḍayaṁ ॥ 73 ॥ 1105 ॥
kōlaulakhaṇiyamōtthāpaēsadīsaṁtaṇihimuhavihāyaṁ । gharabhittisamuṭṭhiyaviḍaviṇivahaṇivaḍaṁtadhavalaharaṁ ॥ 74 ॥1106 ॥
iya ērisaṁ ṇiyaṁtō jā gaccha tāva tassa pāsammi । pēcchai vitthaḍakūvaṁ jalapuṇṇaṁ ēgadēsammi ||75 ||1107 ॥
uttuṁga - paḍiyapāyāravēḍhiyaṁ saḍiyathāṇayatthāṇaṁ । aduggamappavēsaṁ pāyālatalaṁ va gaṁbhīraṁ ॥ 76 ॥1108 ॥

<pb n="134"/>

taṁ daṭṭu āsasiō dīharavallīē baṁdhiuṁ puḍayaṁ । kaḍūḍhēūṇaṁ ṇīraṁ piyai tisāpasamaṇaṭṭāē ॥ 77 ॥ 1109 ॥
kayalaimāiphalēhiṁ kāūṇaṁ taha ya pāṇavittiṁ ca । jāi puṇō vi hu dūrē hiṁḍatō tassa ṇayarassa ॥ 78 ॥ 1110॥
ētthaṁtarammi mittō mittō iva tassa āvaī ṭaṭṭu । paḍikāuṁ acayaṁtō sahasā asaṇaṁ pattō ॥ 79 ॥1111॥
ahavā vi hu paḍiyāraṁ āvaipaḍiyassa kāumacaṁ yaṁtō । maṇṇubharēṇa va sūrō avarasamuddaddahē paḍiō ॥ 80 ॥ 1112 ॥
atthamiyammi ya sūrē jaladāṇatthaṁ va jāi diṇalacchī । kayarattaṁbaravēsā avarasamuddaddahē cēva ॥ 81 ॥ 1113 ॥
sōyabharēṇa'kkaṁtā kayatārāharaṇamukkatamakēsā । ciṭṭhēuṁ acaēṁtī sā vi tahiṁ cēva ṇibbuḍā ॥ 82 ॥ 1114॥
ēvaṁvihē paōsē girivarapāyassa hēṭubhūmīē । aisīēṇa'kkaṁtō pāḍēuṁ jālaē jalaṇaṁ ॥ 83 ॥ 1115 ॥
jā vōlīṇā rayaṇī tāva pabhāyammi jalaṇadēsammi । bhūmiṁ suvaṇṇarūvaṁ daṇaṁ citaē ēvaṁ ॥ 84 ॥ 1116॥
"ṇūṇaṁ suvaṇṇadīvō hōhī ēsō ṇa ēttha saṁdēhō । jēṇa suvaṇṇībhūyaṁ dīsaī ēvaṁ dharaṇikhaṁḍaṁ ॥ 85 ॥ 1117 ॥
pāḍēmi tā suvaṇṇaṁ " ēvaṁ paribhāviūṇa tēṇa kayā । iṭṭāṇaṁ saṁghāḍā pakkā tē jāliuṁ jalaṇaṁ ॥ 86 ॥ 1118 ॥
paribhramamāṇō jā annavāsarē jāi giriṇiguṁjammi । tā rayaṇāgaramēgaṁ pēcchai rayaṇēhiṁ paḍipuṇṇaṁ ॥ 87 ॥ 1119॥
tattō sō rayaṇāī āṇēuṁ dharai iṭṭapāsammi । ēvaṁ kamēṇa tēṇaṁ rayaṇa-suvaṇṇaṁ bahuṁ gahiyaṁ ॥ 88 ॥ 1120॥

tayaṁ dīvaṁ nagariūṇaṁ tahiṁ tayaṁ vahaṇaṁ । pēsai ya ṇiyayapurisē ṇīrassa gavēsaṇa'ṭṭhāē ॥ 90 ॥ 1122 ॥
dahūṇaṁ tē dhaṇayaṁ pucchaṁtī 'kahasu kō tumaṁ ēttha ?' । jaṁpai dhaṇaō 'bhaddaya ! vaṇacaraō ēttha ṇivasāmi ॥91॥ 1123॥
puṭṭō ya tēhiṁ ēsō 'jai ēvaṁ tō jalaṁ payaṁsēhi' । tēṇā'vi hu sō kūbō payaṁsiō viyaḍagaṁbhīrō ॥ 92 ॥ 1124 ॥
tassā'yaḍassa pāsē suvaṇṇa rayaṇāiyaṁ tayaṁ dahuṁ । pucchaṁti 'kassa ēvaṁ iha ciṭui sōhaṇaṁ davyaṁ ? ' ॥ 93 ॥ 1125 ॥
jaṁpai dhaṇaō 'majjha ēyaṁ davyaṁ aīvasumahaṁta । jai nēha imaṁ tā vasimaṁ tubbhaṁ dēmi caubhāyaṁ ॥ 94 ॥ 1126 ॥
tēhiṁ vi bhaṇiyaṁ ēyaṁ 'satthāhō jāṇaī aō tassa । sāhēmō jaṁ cittē paḍihāsai tassa taṁ kuṇau ॥95॥1127॥
' ēvaṁ ' ti tēṇa bhaṇiē gaṁtuṁ sārhēti tē sudattassa । sō vi tayaṁ āyaṇṇiya ēi duyaṁ dhaṇayapāsamma ॥96॥ 1128 ॥
daguṇa satthavāhaṁ ētaṁ abbhuṭuē imō sahasā । kuṇai paṇāmāīyaṁ paḍivattiṁ satthavāhassa ॥97॥1129॥
sō vihu āliṁgēuṁ siddhibaṁdhu vva pucchaē kusalaṁ । bhaṇiō dhaṇaēṇēsō 'maha davvaṁ nēhi basimammi ॥ 98 ॥ 1130 ॥
dēmi cautthaṁ bhāgaṁ' sō vi hu jaṁpēi 'hōu davvēṇaṁ । ṇēmi tumaṁ ēvaṁ ciya kimēttha bahuṇā palattēṇaṁ ? ' ॥99॥1131॥
bhaṇiyā ya kammayārā 'nēha imaṁ majjha pavahaṇē davvaṁ । pāhāṇē chaḍḍittā suvaṇṇayaṁ kuṇaha hāyaṁ' ॥100॥ 1132॥

<pb n="136"/>

tēhiṁ vi 'taha' tti vihiyaṁ saṁbhālittāṇa appiyaṁ tēṇa । rayaṇāṇi ya dhaṇaēṇaṁ kayāṇi guttēsu ṭhāṇēsu ॥ 101 ॥ 1133 ॥
daṭṭuṇa bahu davvaṁ caliyaṁ cittaṁ sudattavaṇiyassa । aha sanniyā ya purisā 'khivaha imaṁ ēttha kūvammi' ॥ 102 ॥ 1134 ॥
tō tēhiṁ dhaṇō bhaṇiō 'kaḍūḍhasu ṇīraṁ ṇa yāṇimō amhē' । jā sō kaḍūḍhai ṇīraṁ tā khittō tēhiṁ ayaḍammi ॥ 103 ॥ 1135॥
paṇṇūramajjhaḍiō maṇayaṁ pi ya nēya pīḍiō dēhē । uṭṭhēi sasaṁbhaṁtō kūvayapāsāī pulayaṁtō ॥104॥1136॥
gāha'tthaṁ ciṁtatō iō taō jāva tattha paribhamai । tā jalarahiyapaēsē pēcchai ēgaṁ mahaduvāraṁ ॥ 105 ॥ 1137॥
jāva ṇirūvēi tayaṁ tā varasōvāṇapatiyaṁ niyai । hēṭṭhāmuhaṁ vayaṁtī avayarai ahōmuhaṁ tīē ॥106 ॥ 1138 ॥
avayariya thōvabhāyaṁ jāi puṇō paṁjalēṇa maggēṇa । pēcchaṁtō āyāsaṁ ṭaṁkichinnē ya giripāsē ॥ 107 ॥ 1139 ॥
āyāsatalavilaggē ubhaō pāsēsu girivarē dahuṁ । ciṁtai “ahaha ! ahō ! hō ! acchariyaṁ kiṁpi naju ēyaṁ ॥108॥। 1140 ॥
ahavā vi kiṁ imēṇaṁ ? puraō pēcchāmi kiṁpi jaṁ hōi " । jā ēva jāi dhaṇaō tā ṇiyai surālayaṁ ēkkaṁ ॥ 109॥1141॥
savvarayaṇāmayaṁ taṁ dahuṁ kōūhalēṇa apphuṇṇō । jā pavisai tā pēcchai majjhē cakkēsarīpaḍimaṁ ॥110॥1142 ॥
daddr̥ṇa tayaṁ haṁṭuō baṁdai gurubhattipulaiyasarīrō । thuṇai ya mahurasarēṇaṁ 'jaya jaya jaya dēvi ! dēvi ! tti ॥ 111॥1143॥
jaya jaya garuḍaṇisaṇṇē ! jaya jaya varacakkasōhiyakaraggē ! । jaya jaya bhūsaṇadhāriṇi ! jaya jaya surasuṁdarīṇamiē ! ॥ 112 ॥1144 ॥
1. paṇṇaura° pā0 ।। 2. tuṭṭō jē0 kā0 ॥

<pb n="137"/>

jaya paṇayakappalaiē ! jaya jaya ciṁtāmaṇīmahādēvi ! । saṁpai maha tuha pāyā saraṇaṁ" bhaṇiuṁ ṇivajē ॥ 113 ॥1145 ॥
bhattīē gahiyahiyayā jaṁpai cakkēsarī 'tumaṁ vaccha ! । vaccasu puraō jēṇaṁ savvaṁ piṁ hu sōhaṇaṁ hōi ॥ 114 ॥1146॥
kiṁca vimaggāhi varaṁ jaṁ tuha cittassa kiṁpiṁ paḍihāi' । bhaṇai imō 'paramēsari ! kimannamēttō vi laṭuyaraṁ ॥ 115 ॥1147 ॥
jaṁ lōyammi vi dulahaṁ taṁ dinnaṁ daṁsaṇaṁ taē majjha । tā sāmiṇi ! jāmi ahaṁ karēmi āṇattiyaṁ tujjha ' ॥ 116 ॥1148 ॥
dēvī vi bhaṇai 'puttaya ! mahappabhāvāī paṁcarayaṇāī । ēyāī gēṇha, jēṇaṁ sahalaṁ maha daṁsaṇaṁ hōī ॥117॥1149 ॥
dāuṁ dhaṇayassa karē jaṁpai cakkēsarī jahā 'vaccha ! । aiṁgaṁ sōhaggakaraṁ, lacchīnilayaṁ imaṁ bīyaṁ ॥ 118 ॥1150 ॥
taiyamimaṁ rōgaharaṁ, cautthayaṁ visaviṇāsaṁyaṁ ēyaṁ । āvaipaḍiyaṁ tu ṇaraṁ ṇitthārai paṁcamaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 119॥1151 ॥
ēyammi majjha vayaṇē na hu saṁdēhō kayāi kāyavvō' । iya jaṁpiūṇa dēvī jhaḍatti ahaṁsaṇihūyā ॥120॥1152॥
cakkēsariṁ ṇamēuṁ dhaṇaō jā jāi aggaōhutaṁ । tā ōsahiṁ niyacchai puraō saṁrōhaṇīṇāma ||121 ॥ 1153॥
taṁ dahūṇaṁ phāḍai ṇiyajaghaṁ thavai tāṇi rayaṇāṇi । ōsahirasēṇa sittaṁ na najaē jhatti vaṇavivaraṁ ॥ 122॥1154॥
ēvaṁ ca karēūṇaṁ baccai puraō pahiduhiyaō sō । pēcchai ya mahārammaṁ pāyālapuraṁ tahiṁ ēkaṁ ॥ 123॥1155॥

jā kōūhalapunnō pavisai tā uvvasaṁtayaṁ niyai । vaccaṁtō ya ṇiyacchai ṇāṇāvihabhakkhapuṇṇāō ॥ 124 ॥1156 ॥
pavarakayāṇayajuttāō paramarammāō vivihavīhīō । ṇimāṇusāō ṇavaraṁ dhavalaharāī pi ya tahēva ॥ 125 ॥ 1157 ॥
pēcchatō rammāī sattatalāī dhaōhakaliyāī । aha annammi paēsē ṇiyai narēṁdassa pāsāyaṁ ॥ 126 ॥ 1158 ॥
uttuṁgasālakaliyaṁ ṇimmiyavarabhavaṇatōraṇaduvāraṁ । pavaragavakkhaya- cōṁpālayāīkaliyaṁ mahārambhaṁ ॥127॥1159 ॥
pavisai ya kōugēṇaṁ ṇariṁdabhavaṇammi taha samāruhai । jā sattamiyaṁ bhūmiṁ tā pēcchai bāliyaṁ ēkkaṁ ॥ 128||1160 ॥
miu-ṇiddha-kasiṇa-kuṁciyakēsa kalāvaṁ sukaṁtamuhacaṁdaṁ । kaṁbusamasarisagīvaṁ uttuṁgapaōharakaṁtaṁ ॥129॥1161॥
sukumāladīhabāhuṁ asōyapallavasamāṇa karajuyalaṁ । vajrasamakhāmamajjhaṁ gaṁbhīrāvattaṇāhillaṁ ॥130||1162 ॥
viyaḍaṇiyaṁba karikarasarisōruṁ cāruēṇiyājaṁghaṁ । kummapaṭṭiyacalaṇaṁ siṇiddhaṇahakiraṇakabburiyaṁ ॥131॥1163॥
taṁ daddr̥ṇaṁ ēsō ciṁtai cittammi “kā imā bālā ? | añccaṁtarūvakaliyā ciṭṭhai ēgāgiṇī ēttha ॥132॥1164॥
tō pucchāmi imaṁ ciya" jāvēvaṁ ciṁtaē taō tīē । bhaṇiō 'hā hā! muddhaya! jōvvaṇa-guṇa-rūvaāvāsa ! ॥ 133 ॥ 1165 ॥
kattha tumaṁ saṁpattō appavahatthā imammi ṭhāṇammi ? । tā ṇiggaccha lahuṁ ciya, jāva viṇāsaṁ ṇa pāvēsi ' ॥134॥1166॥
1. 'isahiyaṁ kā0 ।। 2. suddhi jē0 kā0 ॥
<pb n="139"/>

bhaṇiyā dhaṇēṇa 'suṁdari ! mā ubvēyaṁ karēha, maha sāha । kassa sayāsāō bhayaṁ ? kō vā ēsō paēsō tti ? ॥135॥1167॥
kiṁnāmayaṁ ca ṇayaraṁ ? kiṁ vā vi hu sunnayaṁ amāṇussaṁ ? । iya sāhasa majjha tumaṁ aigaruyaṁ kōuyaṁ jēṇa ' ॥ 136 ॥1168 ॥
tō dhīrattaṇa-sukumālavayaṇarūvēhiṁ raṁjiyā bālā । aha akkhiuṁ payattā 'suṇasu mahābhāga ! jai kōḍuṁ ॥137॥1169॥
" āsi iha bharahabāsē siritilayaṁ ṇāma paṭṭaṇaṁ rammaṁ । tatthā''si piyā majjhaṁ mahēṁdarāō mahārāō ॥ 138 ॥ 1170 ॥
sō annayā kayāī bala - pōrisadappiēhiṁ rāīhiṁ । jā ciṭui akkaṁtō tāva ya kira tassa pāsammi ॥ 139॥ 1171॥
saṁpattō divvavasā ēgō aha vāṇamaṁtarō dēvō । ciṁtai " hā ! kaha ēsō paḍiō kaṭummi ṇaraṇāhō ? || 140॥1172॥
pēcchaṁtassa ya ēyaṁ majjha uppajjaē maṇē tōsō । tā kiṁ kāraṇamēyaṁ sammaṁ jāṇāmi ṇāṇēṇaṁ" || 141 ॥ 1173॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa ṇāṇaṁ vipphārai jāva tāva sō muṇai । “huṁ ēsō puvvabhavē āsī maha aipiō mittō" ॥142॥1174॥
āgaṁtuṁ ṇivapāsē jaṁpai sō 'ṇaravariṁda ! ṇisuṇēhi । atthi iha bharahakhēttē supasiddhaṁ puravaraṁ rammaṁ ॥ 143 ॥ 1175॥
ṇāmēṇa caṁdapuraṁ puravaraguṇarayaṇarōhaṇamahagghaṁ । taṁ paripālai rāyā caṁdajasō ṇāma supasiddhō || 144 | | 1176 ॥
tassa'tthi caṁdakaṁtā dēvī 'tēlōkkaramaṇijiyarūvā । sayalakalāgamakaliyā kamaṇīyā ṇiyayakaṁtassa ॥ 145॥1177॥
1. uvvēvaṁ jē0 kā0 ।। 2. kinnāma tru0 kā0 ॥। 3. tēlukka° jē0 ।।

<pb n="140"/>

ēttō ya tammi ṇayarē aṇēyavaṇisahasaṇāyagō sēṭṭhī । atthi suvikkhāyajasō jiṇadattō ṇāma jiṇabhattō ॥ 146 ॥ 1178 ।।
annō vi tassa mittō tattha purē basai saṁkhadattavaṇī | mēttībhāvamuvagaō accatthaṁ tassa sēṭuissa ॥ 147 ॥ 1179॥
aha annayā kayāī ṇiyahaṭṭē jāva ciṭui ṇiviṭṭhō । tā siddhavihiyavēsō saṁpattō takkarō ēgō ॥ 148 ॥। 1180॥
tēṇa vi vatthaṁtāō chōḍittā rayaṇamēgamairammaṁ । dinnaṁ vaṇiyassa karē ṇāmēṇa saṁkhadattassa ॥149॥1181 ॥
tēṇa viya tayaṁ dahūṁ cittammi vigappiyaṁ jahā ēyaṁ । “dīsai sutēyarayaṇaṁ taṁ mannē hōhii aṇagghaṁ" || 150 | 1182 ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa tēṇaṁ puṭṭhō 'kiṁ dēmi bhadda ! tuha mōllaṁ ? ' । tēṇa vi ya taō bhaṇiyaṁ 'dēhi tayaṁ hōi jaṁ uciyaṁ ' ॥ 151 ॥ 1183 ॥
aha vaṇiēṇa viṇiyaē cittammi viyakkiyaṁ jahā ēsō । “dīsai aīvamuddhō jaṁ kiṁcī dēmi tā mōllaṁ” ॥152॥1184॥
tō dinnā dammāṇaṁ sahassa dasa tēṇa tassa cōrassa । sō tēhiṁ ciya tuṭṭhō vaccai ṇiyayammi ṭhāṇammi ॥ 153 ॥। 1185 ॥
vilasai ya jahicchāē taṁ davvaṁ bahuvihappayārēhiṁ । ēttō ya tattha muṭuṁ bhaṁḍāraṁ kēṇa vi ṇivassa || 154 ॥ 1186॥
tassa ya gavēsaṇatthaṁ bhamai talārō gharāghariṁ jāva । tā hiṁḍatō kamasō saṁpattō tattha ṭhāṇammi || 155 ॥ 1187 ॥
jattha'cchai vilasaṁtō sō cōrō bahuvihāhiṁ kīlāhiṁ । taṁ daddūṇaṁ talārō ciṁtai "davvaṁ imassa kaō ? " ॥ 156 ॥1188 ॥
jāva ya tayaṁ ṇirikkhai tā pēccha cōralakkhaṇaṁ tammi । tē dahūṇaṁ ciṁtai “ṇūṇaṁ ēsō bhavē cōrō ॥157॥1189 ॥
tā baṁdhāvēmi imaṁ jēṇaṁ jāṇāmi sē phuḍaṁ bhāvaṁ" । iya ciṁtiūṇa tēṇaṁ āiṭṭhā ṇiyayapāikkā || 158 ||1190॥

<pb n="141"/>

! rē ! baṁdhēha imaṁ jēṇaṁ jāṇāmi bhāvamēyassa' । tō tē vi takkhaṇaṁ ciya baṁdhaṁti tayaṁ sukuddha vva ॥ 159 ॥ 1191॥
puṭṭhō ya 'kaō tujjhaṁ rē ! rē ! ēvaṁvihā imā lacchī ?' । tēṇā'vi 'jāṇiō' tti ya saccaṁ ciya akkhiyaṁ savvaṁ ॥ 160॥1192॥
pabhaṇai taō talārō 'jai ēvaṁ tō samappasu asēsaṁ' । tēṇa vi vikkiyarayaṇaṁ mōttūṇaṁ appiyamasēsaṁ ॥ 161॥1193 ॥
puṇaravi ya talārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ 'natthēttha ēga maharayaṇaṁ' । jaṁpai imō vi 'dinnaṁ haṭṭē taṁ saṁkhadattassa ' ॥ 162॥1194॥
tō saṁkhadattavaṇiō sahasā giṇhāviō talārēṇaṁ । taṁ ṇāūṇaṁ sēṭṭhī jiṇadattō jāi ṇivapāsē ॥ 163 ॥ 1195 ॥
vinnaviuṁ mēllāvai taṁ vaṇiyaṁ saṁkhadattavaramittaṁ । jāō ya taō suhiō puṇaravi baccaṁta kālē || 164 ॥1196 ॥
sō saṁkhadattavaṇiō vaccai ṇayarassa dūradēsatthē | dēvaulē tatthadviyadēvassa ṇamaṁsaṇaḍāē || 165॥1197॥
aittō ya tammi ṇayarē kuṭuṁbiō basai sōmarāō tti । tassa'tthi varā bhajjā supasiddhā rūviṇī nāma ॥ 166 ॥1198 ॥
sā āsattā ahiyaṁ rēvaṇanāmammi annapurisammi । jāṇai ya sōmarāō jahā viṇaṭuṁ imaṁ kannaṁ ॥ 167 ॥ 1199 ॥
bujhai ya ṇataṁ purisaṁ, vaha ya khēyaṁ maṇammi anbhahiyaṁ । ciṁtai ya bahūvāēṁ jārassa viyāṇaṇaṭṭāē ॥168॥ 1200 ॥
sā vi ya tammi suragihē paidiyahaṁ jāi vihiyasaṁkēyā । tammi diṇammi ṇa pattō kahamavi sō rēvaṇō tattha ॥ 169॥1201॥ .
1. bhō ! baṁdhēha kā0 ।। 2. gēvhā jē0 ॥। 3. vinnaviya truo || 4. 'dēsamma kā0 ।। 5. tatō jē0 ।। 6. °ē parapurisavi' jē0 ।।

pattō ya saṁkhadattō, divvavasā hēriyāya tammi dinē । diṭṭhō ya saṁkhadattō pavitō sōmarāēṇa ॥ 170 ॥ 1202 ॥
kōvāyaṁbiraṇayaṇēṇa tēṇa sahasa tti tō imō gahiō । bhaṇiō ya 'kattha vaccasi rē pāva ! imaṁ karēmāṇō ? ' ॥ 171 ॥ 1203 ॥
baṁdhittu āṇiō ṇaravaissa pāsammi sōmarāēṇa । nāūṇa tayaṁ sahasā samāgaō sēṭṭhī jiṇadattō ॥ 172 ॥1204॥
puṭṭhō ya sēṭṭhiṇā sō 'kammāṇa imāṇa kāraō kiṁ taṁ ? ' । sō jaṁpai 'mitta ! ahaṁ maṇasā vi imaṁ ṇa ciṁtēmi ॥ 173॥1205॥
jaṁi ṇa vi pattiyaha mahaṁ pattijjāvēmi tō ahaṁ ṇiyamā । ṭuḍēṇa vi divvēṇaṁ saṁdēhō ṇatthi ētthatthē ' ॥174 ॥ 1206 ॥
tō ṇaravaissa puraō sēṭṭī jaṁpai viṇicchyaṁ kāuṁ । 'dēva ! imō ṇa hu kārī, giṇhai duṭuṁ pi jaṁ divvaṁ' ॥175॥। 1207 ॥
bhaṇai ṇivō 'maha divvaṁ tuha vayaṇaṁ cēva, kiṁ viyappēṇa ?" । ēvaṁ ca mōiūṇaṁ āṇai sēṭṭī tayaṁ gēhē ॥ 176 ॥ 1208 ॥
baddhāvaṇayaṁ kāuṁ, ciṁtai aha saṁkhadattaṇāmō vi । "pēccha adōsō vi ahaṁ viḍaṁbiō naṇu kahaṁ vihiṇā ॥ 177॥1209॥
tā pajattaṁ majjha imēṇa ēvaṁvihēṇa gēhēṇa" । iya ciṁtiūṇa gahiyā parivāyagasaṁtiyā dikkhā || 178 ॥ 1210॥
parivāliūṇa dikkhaṁ saṁjāō vāṇamaṁtarō dēvō । tattō caviūṇa puṇō saṁsāraṁ hiṁḍiuṁ kiṁci ॥ 179 ॥ 1211॥
tattō ya puvvajammē kiṁci tavaṁ kariya puṇa surō jāō । ahayaṁ jō tujjha imō paccakkhō rāya ! ciṭṭhāmi ॥180॥1212 ॥

jiṇadattō vi hu tattō mariuṁ sōhammadēvalōgammi । uvavannō tiyasavarō tattō caviuṁ tumaṁ jāō ॥ 181॥ 1213।
tā taṁ daddūṇamahaṁ puṇaravi nēhō daḍhaṁ imō jāō । 'tā tuha karēmi kimahaṁ paramuvagārissa mittassa ? ॥ 182 ॥1214॥
taha vi hū kēhēhi supurisa ! kajjuṁ maha atthi kiṁci jai jōgaṁ' । rannā vitaō laviyaṁ 'cauddisiṁ vēḍhiō ahayaṁ ॥ 183 ।। 1215 ॥
aibalavayasattūhiṁ tā ēttha karēhi kiṁci sāhējaṁ'। jaṁpai imō vi 'ṇaravara ! ṇatthi ya ēsā mahaṁ sattī ॥ 184 ॥ 1216 ॥
jamhā baliyasurēhiṁ ahiṭṭiyā sattuṇō imē tujjha । kiṁtu tuhaṁ sāhēja karēmi duggaṁ payaṁsittā' ॥185॥1217॥
tō savyatiriya-ra-ṇārisaṁjuyaṁ āṇiūṇa iha ṭhāṇē । jhatti ṇivēsai ēyaṁ ṇayaraṁ pāyālapuraṇāmaṁ ॥ 186॥ 1218॥
acaṁtagūḍhaniggamapavēsajuttaṁ jaō ihaṁ ēgaṁ । kūvayamajjhaduvāraṁ taō ya kūvāō ṇiggamaṇaṁ ॥ 187॥1219॥
sōvāṇapaṁtiyāē tattō uvariṁ ṇivēsiyaṁ tattha । kūvayarakkhaṇahēuṁ puṇō vi varapaṭṭaṇaṁ annaṁ ॥ 188 || 1220॥
vahaṇēhiṁ tattha ṇāṇāvihāraṁ āvaṁti bhōgaaṁgāī । tattō pavisaṁti ihaṁ hōi taō sutthiō lōgō ॥ 189॥1221॥
ēvaṁ ca kēttiō vi hu jā kālō jāi muiyacittāṇaṁ । tā āgāsagamēṇaṁ pattō vijjāharō ēgō ॥ 190॥1222॥
dīharapalaṁba kuccō dīhabhuō viyaḍavaccha pihujaṁghō । māṇusamaṁsapa iṭṭō ṇicaṁ pi viṇāsaē lōyaṁ ॥ 191 ।1223॥

<pb n="144"/>

kūvayapavēsasōvāṇapaṁtiyaṁ bhaṁjiūṇa sō pāvō । bhakkhara diyahē diyahē rakkhasarūvī maṇussāī ॥192॥1224॥
ēvaṁ bhakkhatēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ uvvāsiyaṁ puraṁ ēyaṁ । mōttūṇa mamaṁ ēgaṁ annō iha māriō lōgō ॥193॥। 1225 ॥
bāhirapuraṁ pi pāvēṇa jāva aṁha bhakkhiuṁ samādattaṁ । vahaṇēsu āruhittā tā ṇaṭṭō sēsaō lōgō ॥ 194 ॥ 1226॥
ēsō vi annadēsaṁtarāṇa paidiyaha māriuṁ lōyaṁ । bhakkhara vijābaliō paccakkhō rakkhasō jāō ॥ 195 ॥ 1227 ॥
ēttō ya sattamadiṇē ēēṇaṁ akkhiyaṁ mahaṁ ēyaṁ । jaha ṇisuṇasu varabālē ! maha vayaṇaṁ avahiyā hōuṁ ॥ 196 ॥1228॥
'ētō vēyaḍḍhanagē atthi puraṁ rayaṇasaṁcayaṁ nāma । tatthā''si ahaṁ rāyā nāmēṇaṁ pavaṇavēgō tti ॥197॥1229 ॥
māṇusamaṁsē ya mahaṁ saṁjāyaṁ dāruṇaṁ mahāvasaṇaṁ । tō 'rakkhasō 'tti kāuṁ tatttō ṇivvāsiō ahayaṁ ॥ 198॥1230॥
pattō ya ēttha ṇayarē ēvaṁ pi hu bhakkhiyaṁ maē savvaṁ । 'airūviṇi' tti kāuṁ ēkka cciya rakkhiyā taṁ si ॥ 199॥1231॥
ēttō ya sattamadiṇē pariṇissaṁ taṁ subhammi laggammi । bhuṁjissāmi ya bhōē tumaē samayaṁ ahaṁ muddhē !' ॥ 200॥1232॥
ēyaṁ ca ahaṁ sōuṁ vajrēṇa samāhaya vva saṁjāyā । maraṇassa ya bīhaṁtī tavvayaṇaṁ manniuṁ thakkā ॥ 201 ॥1233॥
ajaṁ ca tassa diyahō vaṭṭai sō sattamō aō jāva । nā''gacchai sō pāvō tā jīyaṁ tujjha takkēmi ॥ 202॥1234॥
pāṇēhiṁtō vi tumaṁ suṁdara ! maha vallahō aō jāyaṁ । duguṇayaraṁ maha hiyaē mahābhayaṁ tivvaduhasahiyaṁ ॥ 203॥1235॥
1. iha pā0 ।। 2. yaḍūḍhapurē a' pā0 ॥। 3. hāsukkhaṁ jē0 ॥

tā sigdhaṁ gaccha tumaṁ jēṇāgamaṇassa baṭṭaē samaō । rakkhassa tassa" ēvaṁ bhaṇiē dhaṇaō payaṁpēi ॥ 204॥1236॥
' mā suṁdari ! bīha tumaṁ, ajaṁ mārēmi taṁ durāyāraṁ । khēmaṁ karēmi ṇiyamā savvassa vi jīvalōgassa' ॥205॥1237॥
ēvaṁ sōuṁ jaṁpai 'jai kāyavyaṁ imaṁ taē sāmi ! । tō ṇisuṇa tassa mammaṁ jēṇa suhēṇaṁ vivāḍēsi ॥ 206॥1238॥
vijjāō pūyaṁtō ṇa ēsa jaṁpēi, ṇēya uḍēi । bajē vi huṁ ṇivaḍaṁtē tā ghāyasu tammi samayammi || 207|| 1239॥
ēyaṁ ca majjha jaṇayassa saṁtiyaṁ ciṭuē mahākhaggaṁ । giṇhēyavvaṁ tumaē sāmiya ! kāuṁ dayaṁ majjha ॥ 208॥1240॥
ēvaṁ ca jā payaṁpai tāvēsō āgaō gahiyapurisō । dahuṁ dhaṇayaṁ sahasā pahasaṁtō jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ॥ 209॥1241॥
'ahaha ! ahō ! acchariyaṁ, bhakkhaṁ maha āgayaṁ sayaṁ cēva' । iya bhaṇiuṁ rīḍhāē mēllai jaṁ āṇiyaṁ maḍayaṁ ॥ 210 | 1242 ॥
pūēuṁ vijjāō jāva pavattō taō imēṇā'vi । āyaḍriḍhaūṇa khaggaṁ aha sahasā hakkaō ēsō ॥211॥1243 ॥
'rē ! rē! rakkhasa ! pāvaya ! ṇillajjaya! aiaṇajja ! narabhakkha ! । aja ṇa hōsi khaṇēṇaṁ maha hatthāō ṇa saṁdēhō ॥ 212॥1244॥
tā uṭusu karasu karē khaggaṁ ṇāsēmi jēṇa tuha dappaṁ' । iya bhaṇiō'banāē hasiuṁ pūēi bijāō ॥ 213 ॥1245 ॥
pūēuṁ vijjāō jā uṭui tā imēṇa sahasa tti । khaggapahārēṇa lahuṁ ṇivāḍiyaṁ bhūyalē sīsaṁ ॥214॥1246॥

<pb n="146"/>

tēṇēva ya vihiyāē sāmaggīē vivāhiyā ēsā । nāmēṇa tilayasuṁdarikannā accaṁtarūyavaī ॥ 215 ॥1247॥
bhuṁjai ya tattha bhōē tīē samaṁ jāva vāsarē kaivi । tāva imīē bhaṇiō 'piyayama ! kiṁ ēttha acchāmō ? ॥ 216 ॥1248॥
maggēṇa kēṇa tumayaṁ samāgaō ? kahasu jēṇa vaccāmō' । iya puṭṭhō tīē dhaṇō kahēi savvaṁ ṇiravasēsaṁ ॥ 217॥1249॥
tō bhai imā 'sāmiya ! baccāmō tattha caiva kūvammi । gahiūṇaṁ saṁvalayaṁ annaṁ pihu jaṁ aṇagdhēyaṁ' ॥218॥ 1250 ॥
paḍibajjiūṇa ‘ēvaṁ' ti sō vi ghēttuṁ pahāṇarayaṇāī । taha tilayasuṁdaraṁ pi ya baccai cakkēsarībhavaṇē ॥ 219॥1251॥
vaṁdittu bhayavaī tō vaccai aha kūvayassa dārammi । mēllittu tahiṁ bhajaṁ āṇai annaṁ pi suṁdarayaṁ ॥ 220 ॥ 1252॥
kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ ? jaṁ jaṁ cittassa kiṁpi paḍihāi । taṁ taṁ savvaṁ pi tahiṁ āṇēuṁ dhāriyaṁ tēṇa ॥ 221 ॥ 1253॥
jā acchai kē vi diṇē tāva samuddammi āgayaṁ vahaṇaṁ । ṇīraṇimittēṇa puṇō samāgaṁyā kē vi tattha ṇarā ॥ 222 ॥ 1254॥
jā pakkhittō caḍasō, hatthē ghēttūṇa jaṁpaī dhaṇaō । 'bhō ! bhō ! kūvē paḍiō ahayaṁ, uttāraha mamaṁ' ti ॥ 223 ॥1255॥
tēhiṁ pi satthavāhassa akkhiyaṁ dēvadattaṇāmassa । kōugavasēṇa ēsō vi āgaō tattha ṭhāṇammi ॥ 224॥1256 ॥
baṁdhintu varattāē pakkhittā maṁciā taō tīē । āruhiuṁ dhaṇaō vi hu samāgaō kūvayassuvariṁ ॥ 225 ॥ 1257॥
dahūṇa satthavāhō varavatthā - SSharaṇabhūsiyasarīraṁ । ukkidurūvajōvvaṇasamanniyaṁ vimhayaṁ pattō ॥ 226 ॥1258॥

puṭṭhō ya 'kōṇu ? kaha vā tumaṁ ti kūvammi ṇivaḍiō ? kahasu' । sō jaṁpai 'annā vihu ciṭui maha bhāriyā ēttha ॥ 227॥1259॥
annaṁ pi kiṁpi jaladēvayāē dinnaṁ tahēva rayaṇāī । uttāriyammi tammi u kahēmi vīsatthaō savvaṁ ॥ 228 ॥ 1260॥
satthāhō vihu aha vimhayāulō bhaṇai 'kuṇasu ēvaṁ 'ti । tēṇa vi bhaṇiyā ēsā 'piē! caḍāvēhi savvamiṇaṁ ॥ 229॥1261॥
uttāriyammi savvammi tammi pacchā sayaṁ pi uttinnā । daṭṭhūṇa dēvadattō ciṁtai “kiṁ dēvayā ēsā ? ॥230॥1262॥
ēsō vi kavi dēvō hōhī nūṇaṁ" ti jā palōēi । tā dōṇha vi acchīō kuṇaṁti ummēsa - ṇimmēsē ॥231॥1263 ॥
ṇāyaṁ ca tāva tēṇaṁ "ṇa hōṁti ēyāṇi dō vi dēvāṇi । vijjāharāṇi tā kiṁ ? ahavā ēyaṁ pi ṇa ghaḍēi ॥ 232॥1264॥
jamhā hu kūvayāō sayaṁ ṇa sakkaṁti ṇīsarēūṇaṁ । ahavā u avaharēuṁ [graṁthāgra 2000 ] ṇūṇaṁ vijjāō kēṇā'vi ॥ 233 ॥ 1265॥
khittāṇi kūvayammi pubvavirudvēṇa dēvarūvēṇa । ahavā vi kiṁ imēṇaṁ ? pucchāmi imaṁ mahābhāgaṁ " ॥ 234 ॥ 1266 ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa tēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ 'uvavisasu tā mahābhāga ! । kahiuṁ ṇiyavuttaṁtaṁ saṁdēhaṁ majjha avaṇēhi ' ॥ 235 ॥1267॥

tuṭṭēṇa taō rannā bhaṇiō macchōyarō ' jahēyassa । dēhi sayaṁ taṁbōlaṁ gaṁdhavviyarayaṇabhūyassa ॥ 308 ॥ 1340 ॥
gīyaraissa' taō sō taṁbōlaṁ jāva dēi dūratthō । tā 'bhāi ! bhāi ! bhāi !' tti jaṁpirō laggaē kaṁḍē ॥ 309 ॥ 1341 ॥
puṭṭhō ya ṇaravarēṇaṁ 'gaṁdhavviya ! kiṁ taē imaṁ vihiyaṁ ? ' । sō hi payaṁpai 'sāmiya ! ēsō maha hōi bhāi tti ॥ 310॥1342॥
bahuyāṇaṁ divasāṇaṁ ēsō miliō maē ya vinnāō । ēēṇaṁ ciṁdhēṇaṁ dāhiṇapāyaṭṭiēṇa'ja' ॥311 ॥1343 ॥
tā savvaṁ pi kuṭuṁbaṁ kaṁḍē ghēttūṇa rōviyaṁ tassa । rannā vi imō puṭṭhō 'macchōyara ! kiṁ imaṁ saccaṁ ? ' ॥312|| 1 344 ॥
iyarēṇa vi ṇiyahiyaē kavaḍamiṇaṁ bhāviūṇa saṁlattaṁ । 'dēva ! imaṁ ēvaṁ ciya saccaṁ natthēttha saṁdēhō ' ॥ 313॥1345 ॥
tō pāusaṇahayalamiva rannā aṁdhāriyaṁ ṇiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ । 'hā hā hā ! pāvēṇaṁ kaha maha viṭṭhāliyaṁ gēhaṁ ' ॥314॥1346॥
kōvāyaṁbiravayaṇēṇa bhāṇiyaṁ rē ! imaṁ viṇāsēha । vaṇiō tti bhāṇiūṇaṁ jēṇa ahaṁ vaṁciō ēvaṁ ' ॥315॥1347 ॥
macchōyarō papaī 'naraṇāyaga ! suṇasu ēgaviṇṇattiṁ । pacchā jaṁ tuha rōyai taṁ savvaṁ kāravējjāsi ॥ 316 ॥ 1348॥
dēvēttha amha jaṇaō ṇaravaigēhēsu āsi vikkhāō । 'mahagāyaṇō' tti kāuṁ pāvēṁtō bahuvihapasāē ॥317॥ 1349 ॥

dēva ! maṇāgamaṇiṭṭā maha māyā āsi tēṇa kajrēṇa । ahamavi na sammamiṭṭō, ēsō puṇa vallahō ahiyaṁ ॥319॥ 1351 ॥
sō ya aṇāgayadaṁsī amhāṇaṁ āsi saṁtiō tāō । tā jōga - khēmahēuṁ maha jaṁghaṁ phāliuṁ tēṇa ॥ 320 ॥ 1 352 ॥
khiviūṇa paṁcarayaṇāī sāmi ! saṁrōhaṇīē rōhēuṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ āvaikālē bhakkhējasu putta ! ēyāī ॥ 321 ॥ 1353॥
ēyassa puṇō dēhaṁ savvēsu vi maṁsalē ṭhāṇēsu । bhariyaṁ vararayaṇāṇaṁ 'iḍāē suō' tti kāūṇaṁ ॥ 322 ॥1354 ॥
jai dēva ! imaṁ micchā tō pañcakkhaṁ karēmi savvēsiṁ' । iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ jaṁgha phālittā kaḍūḍhaī rayaṇē ॥ 323 ॥ 1355॥
daṁsēi ya savvēsiṁ bhaṇai ya tā ' gēṇha ēyadēhāō । vararaṁ yaṇāī pacchā karēja jaṁ tujjha paḍihāī' ॥ 324॥1356॥
tō rāyā vimhaiō jaṁpa rē ! ēyasaṁtiyaṁ dēhaṁ । cīrēuṁ cīrēuṁ kaḍūḍhaha tā savvarayaṇāī || 325 || 1357 ॥
pacchā jaṁ kira juttaṁ hōhī taṁ cēva ēttha kāhāmō' । iya bhaṇiē gīyaraī baddhō sahasa tti purisēhiṁ ॥ 326॥ 1358॥
virasāī ārasaṁtō āḍhattō cīriuṁ cara carassa । ruhiraṁ mōttūṇa taō ṇa hu annaṁ kiṁpi ṇīharai ॥ 327॥1359 ॥

ēēṇaṁ pāvēṇaṁ satthāhēṇaṁ ahaṁ imaṁ savvaṁ । kāraviō dāūṇaṁ iṭṭāṇaṁ saṁpuḍē caurō ॥ 329॥1361 ॥

jē tē maha gēhammi ciṭṭhati suvaṇṇaiṭṭasaṁghāḍā । jai ṇa vi ēvaṁ ēvaṁ tō pēcchasu sāmi ! āṇēuṁ ॥ 332 ॥ 1364 ॥

bhaṇai imō 'jai savvaṁ pucchasi tā ēttha pavahaṇē dēva ! । maha kaṇayasaṁpuḍasayā aṭu savāyā dhuvaṁ asthi ॥ 335 ॥1367॥
rayaṇāṇaṁ ca sahassā paṇṇārasa divvatēyajuttāṇaṁ । iya ṇāūṇaṁ saṁpai jaṁ kāyavvaṁ tayaṁ kuṇasu' ॥ 336 ॥ 1368 ॥

tō tē ḍōṁbagihāō āṇīē saṁpuḍē palōēi । na ya niyai dhaṇayaṇāmaṁ utthallitō vi savvattō ॥ 341 ॥ 1373 ॥
ullavai ṇivō 'ṇa hu kiṁpi ṇāmayaṁ bhadda ! ēttha pēcchāmō' । bhaṇai sudattō 'saccaṁ ōlakkhāṇaṁ imaṁ dēva ! ' ॥ 342॥1374॥
jaṁpai dhaṇaō 'sāmiya ! na ēyamaliyaṁ jaō vihāḍēuṁ । jōēha jēṇa pēcchaha maha ṇāmaṁkaṁ ṇa saṁdēhō' ॥343॥1375॥
saṁdhīō vihāḍēṁtī jā tā pēcchaṁti nāmayaṁ payaḍaṁ । tō palayakālasarisō kuviō vaṇiyassa ṇaraṇāhō || 344 ॥ 1376 ॥
jaṁpai 'sūlāē imaṁ ārōvaha pāvakāriṇaṁ cōraṁ । ḍōṁba pi hu khairaṁ piva kuṭṭaha iya dōsasaṁjaṇayaṁ ॥ 345 ॥1377॥
ēyaṁ ca mahābhāgaṁ pahāvaha sōvaṇṇiēhiṁ kalasēhiṁ' । iya bhaṇiyammi payaṁpai sahasā macchōyarō 'dēva ! ॥ 346 ॥1378 ॥
jai amhāṇaṁ uvariṁ sapasāō kuṇasi taha ya kāruṇṇaṁ । tō muṁcasu dō vi imē niyapāvabharēṇa viddaviē' ॥347॥1379 ॥
bhaṇai ṇivō 'ṇa hu juttaṁ ēvaṁ ēvaṁvihaṁ karēṁtāṇaṁ । tahavi hu ṇa tujjha paṇayaṁ annaha kāuṁ pariccaēmi' ॥ 348 ॥ 1380 ॥
iya jaṁpiyammi macchōyarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ 'mahāpasāō' tti । dāuṁ cautthabhāyaṁ dhaṇaō vi visajaē vaṇiyaṁ ॥ 349 ॥1381 ॥
ḍōṁbassa vi jaṁ uciyaṁ taṁ dāūṇaṁ taō ṇariṁdassa । ēgatē ṇiyacariyaṁ savvaṁ pi savittharaṁ kahai ।। 350॥1382 ॥
'jaha dēva ! tujjha sēḍissa saṁtiō rayaṇasāraṇāmassa । puttō haṁ' iccāī macchayagilaṇāipajaṁtaṁ ॥ 351 ॥ 1383 ॥

kiṁtu na sāmiya ! ēvaṁ gujjhaṁ kassā'vi pāyaḍēyavvaṁ । jāva ṇa sō saṁpattō' bhaṇai ṇivō 'hōu ēvaṁ ' ti ॥ 353 ॥। 1385 ॥
aha annammi diṇammiṁ pūriyagurusiḍasamūharamaṇīyaṁ । bahudhaya- mālavamālaṁ dīsai āvaṁtayaṁ vahaṇaṁ ॥ 354 ॥ 1386 ॥
taṁ daṭṭuṇaṁ lōgō udghāvai tassa sammuhaṁ jhatti । pēcchaṁtāṇaṁ ca khaṇēṇa āgayaṁ jalahitīrammi ॥ 355॥1387॥
saṁvariyā ya barasiḍā ṇivāḍiyā taha ya kūvayakkhaṁbhā । jalamajjhammi u ṇaṁgarasilāō khittāō mahaīō ॥ 356 ॥ 1388 ॥
baddhāō pāyāō dharaṇayāṇammi aha dharēūṇaṁ । uttariō satthāhō sapariyaṇō dēvadattō sō ॥ 357 ।। 1389 ।।
uttāriyā ya taha tilayasuṁdarī paḍauḍīō uviyāō । uttāriyaṁ ca bhaṁḍaṁ saṁkhitaṁ ṇivaṇarēhiṁ ॥ 358 ॥1390॥
bhariūṇaṁ rayaṇāṇaṁ varathālaṁ tilayasuṁdarīsahiō । saṁpattō ṇivabhavaṇē pavisai ṇaraṇāha'ṇunnāō ॥ 359 ॥ 1391॥
appē pāhuḍaṁ sō uvavisaī āsaṇammi dinnammi । nāyaṁ ca naravarēṇaṁ “dhaṇayakkhāō imō hōhī ॥ 360 ॥ 1 3 92 ।।
jamhā pāsē ēyassa dīsaē kā vi suṁdarā bālā । aṁguṭṭiiyavayaṇā lajjābharamaṁtharasarīrā ॥361॥ 1393॥
taṁ mannē sā ēsā hōhī dhaṇayassa rūviṇī bhajjā" । iya ciṁtiūṇa rāyā saṁbhāsai satthavāhaṁ taṁ ॥ 362 ॥ 1394॥
jaha 'kattō iha tubbhē ? kiṁ vā vi hu bāliyā imā ēttha । āṇīyā ?' iya bhaṇiē satthāhō jaṁpaē ēvaṁ || 363॥1395॥
'dēva ! kaḍāhāō ahaṁ saṁpattō ēttha vavaharaṇahēuṁ । bālā ya imā laddhā samuddamajjhammi dīvammi ॥ 364 ॥ 1396 ॥

tā dēva ! puhaiṇāhā tubbhē iha saṁpayaṁ aō majjha । aṇumannaha jēṇa imā saṁjāyai bhāriyā pavarā' ॥ 365॥1397॥
sōūṇa tayaṁ rāyā saṁpucchai tilayasuṁdaraṁ 'bhaddē ! । kiṁ rōyai tuha ēsō bhattārō satthavāhasuō ?' ॥ 366॥ 1398 ॥
sā bhaṇai 'dēva ! ēsō kayagdhasirasēharō mahāpāvō । ṇillō aidhiṭṭhō addaṭubyō supurisāṇaṁ ॥ 367॥1399 ॥
kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ ? ṇāmaṁ pi hu mā laējjaha imassa । jēṇa guṇarayaṇakhāṇī rūvēṇaṁ vijiyakaṁdappō ॥ 368 ॥ 1400 ॥
sūrō dhīrō suhaō cāī saralō kayaṇṇuō saccō । dakkhinnajuō mēttīpaḍibannō duducittēṇaṁ ॥ 369॥। 1401 ॥
maha rūvamōhiēṇaṁ samuddamajjhammi dēva ! pakkhittō । maha daiō bhaṇiyā haṁ 'suṁdari ! paḍivajasu mamaṁ' ti ॥ 370 ॥। 1402 ॥
tā dēva ! imassa maē dinnaṁ paccuttaraṁ jahā jai maṁ । dāhī rāyā tō haṁ bhajjā hōhāmi iya bhaṇiē ॥371॥1403॥
na kaō imēṇa majjha sīlaviṇāsō aō paraṁ tubhē । kaḍūḍhāvaha maha kaṭṭē, sāhēmi huyāsaṇaṁ jēṇa ॥ 372 ॥ 1404 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca naravarēṇaṁ ' mā pavisa huyāsaṇammi ruddamma । taṁ cēva dēmi tujjha bhattāraṁ dēvayādinnaṁ' ॥ 373॥1405॥
tō bhai imā 'sāmiya! payapālō taṁ si, kīsa luddhō si । dīṇāṇa aṇāhāṇaṁ saraṇēṇaṁ kuṇasi kāruṇṇaṁ ' ॥ 374 ॥ 1406 ॥
bhaṇai ṇivō 'mā vacchē ! maṁgulacittaṁ mamaṁ viyappēhi । dhūyā ya ajapabhidaṁ taṁ majjha na ēttha saṁdēhō || 375॥1407॥
saccaṁ ca bhaṇāmi ahaṁ, tubbhaṁ taṁ cēva dēmi bhattāraṁ ' । sā bhaṇai 'tāya ! ēvaṁ vayaṇaṁ dūraṁ visaṁvayai ॥ 376॥1408॥
kaha sōcci mē bhattā jō pakkhittō mahāsamuddammi ?' । tō taṁbōlachalēṇaṁ dhaṇayaṁ uṭuvai ṇaraṇāhō ॥ 377 ॥ 1409 ॥

bhaṇiyā ya 'putti ! ēyaṁ sayaṁ nirūvēhi hōi kiṁ ēsō । tuha bhattā ? ' iya bhaṇiē uvarimahuttaṁ palōēi ॥ 378 ॥1410॥
bhaṇai ya 'ghaḍai saricchō, kiṁtu saricchāṇa pūriyā puhaī । kaha sō saṁbhāvijjai jō pakkhittō jalaṇihimmi ? ' ॥ 379॥1411॥
iya bhaṇiē bhai imō 'ēīē dēva ! hōi sō bhattā । jō dhavalaharaḍiyāē atakkiō āgaō sahasā ॥ 380 ॥ 1412 ॥
jēṇa ya puṭṭhā ēsā kā si tumaṁ ? kiṁ ca paṭṭaṇaṁ ēyaṁ ? । jassa imīē kahiyaṁ mahiṁdayāī asē pi ॥ 381 ॥ 1413॥
jassa ya imīē kahiyaṁ rakkhasamammaṁ, samappiyaṁ khaggaṁ । nihaō ya jaiṇa rakkhō, jēṇa ya vīvāhiyā tattha ॥ 382॥1414॥
ṇīsāriyā ya kūvāō jēṇa rayaṇāiēhiṁ saṁjuttā । ārōviyā ya vahaṇē, khittō jō jalahimajjhammi ॥ 383 ॥ 1415 ॥
sō hōi dhavō ēīē dēva !' sōuṁ imaṁ taō bālā । ukkaṁṭaiyā sahasā dhārā haiyanīma kusumaṁ va ॥ 384 ॥1416 ॥
ukkaṁḍiyā ya ēsā jalayaravā''yannaṇāō mōri vva । mannē sā varabālā jhaḍatti anna vya saṁjāyā || 385 || 1417 ||
pabhaṇaiya 'tāya ! ēsō sō cēva ya ṇatthi ēttha saṁdēhō । kahamavi maha punnēhiṁ jalanihimajjhāō uttinnō ॥ 386 ॥ 1418 ॥
tā tāya ! tāyabhāvō tumaē ajaṁ payāsiō majjha । vihiō mahāpasāō āisasu jamēttha kāyavvaṁ ॥ 387 ॥ 1419॥

sōūṇa imaṁ macchōyarēṇa calaṇēsu ṇivaḍiuṁ rāyā। vinnattō 'dēva ! mahaṁ khamiyabbō ēsa avarāhō ॥ 390 ॥ 1422 ॥
ubagārī ya mamēsō jēṇaṁ maha piyayamā samāṇīyā । akkhaṁḍiyavaya-sīlā tā muṁcaha savvahā ēvaṁ ' ॥391॥1423॥

iya jaṁpiyammi ēsō 'mahāpasāō tti dēva !' paḍibhaṇai । dāūṇaṁ chanbhāyaṁ visajjiō tēṇa satthāhō ॥ 393 ॥। 1425 ।।
savyaṁ aṇannasarisaṁ tamalaṁkārāi āṇiyaṁ tēṇa । ṇivabhavaṇē taṁ daddhuṁ rāyā ciṁtēi vimhaiō ॥ 394॥1426॥
" ēyassa kaē ēyārisassa taha bāliyāē ēyāē । satthāhō jamakajjaṁ kuṇaī kō tattha saṁdēhō ? " ॥ 395॥1427॥
bhajjappaiyāṇa puṇō parōpparaṁ mēliyammi jaṁ sōkkhaṁ । taṁ jai muṇaṁti tāṇi ya ahavā savvaṇṇuṇāhō tti ॥ 396 ॥1428 ॥
virahāurāṇa ṇavajōvyaṇāṇa rattāṇa mēlaē jāē। jaṁ saṁkappayasōkkhaṁ taṁ kiṁra kō banniuṁ tarai ? ॥397॥1429॥

tattō bīyammi dinē vinnattō naravaī 'imaṁ tēṇaṁ । saṁpai jaṇaēṇa samaṁ ōlakkhāṇaṁ pahu ! karēmi ॥ 399॥ 1431॥

rāēṇa aṇunnāō taṁbōliyamāi bhūriparivārō । jāi jaṇayassa gēhē taṁ daṇuō sēṭṭhī ॥400॥1432।।
dāūṇa āsaṇavarē uvavēsai paramaviṇayasaṁjuttō । vinnavai jōḍiyakarō 'jē kāyavvaṁ tamāisaha || 401 || 1433॥
pūgāiēṇa kēṇa vi kajaṁ tumhāṇa jēṇa taṁ dēmi । gēṇhaha imaṁ gihaṁ pi hu savvaṁ tumhāṇa āyattaṁ ' ॥ 402 ॥1434॥
iya japatō sēṭṭhī gauravavayaṇēhiṁ, jaṁpai imō vi । 'tāya ! imaṁ tuha gēhaṁ saccaṁ savvaṁ mamāyattaṁ ॥ 403॥1435॥
jēṇa ahaṁ tu puttō hōmi aputtassa, kiṁ viyappēṇa ? । pucchāmi kiṁtu ēkkaṁ tuha puttō āsi jō dhaṇaō ॥ 404॥1436॥
sō kattha saṁpai gaō ? ciṭui vā kattha ? kērisō vā vi ? । rūvēṇaṁ vēsēṇaṁ vaēṇa vannēṇa va sarēṇa ॥ 405 ॥ 1437॥
asthi va kāvi hu vattā ? savvaṁ maha kahaha kāraṇaṁ kiṁpi । uddisiūṇaṁ pucchāmi' jēṇa tō jaṁpaē sēṭṭhī ॥ 406॥1438 ॥
'puttaya ! tēṇaṁ gāhā gahiyā dīṇārasaha samōllēṇa । kajrēṇa tēṇa sō kiṁci pharusiō mē ahannēṇa ॥ 407॥1439॥
taṁ ahimāṇaṁ kāuṁ ṇiggaṁtūṇaṁ gharāō akahiṁtō । kattha va gaō ? kahiṁ vā ciṭui ? ēyaṁ na yāṇāmi ॥ 408 ॥। 1440 ॥
rūvāiēhiṁ taṁ ciya paccakkhō hōsi putta ! ṇibrbhataṁ । bahusārikkhā puhaī, tēṇaṁ na bhaṇāmi sō taṁ si' ॥ 409 ॥1431॥
iya jaṁpiyammi jaṁpai dhaṇaō jaha 'tāya ! hōmi ṇibhaṁtaṁ । sō cēva tumha puttō ahayaṁ jōēhi ciṁdhāī' ॥410॥1442 ॥
ēva bhaṇiē ya sēṭṭhī dāhiṇapāyassa saṁtiyaṁ ciṁdhaṁ । sumarittu jā palōyai tā taṁ payaḍaṁ niyacchēi ॥ 411 ॥1443॥
1. hassamō kā0 ॥। 2. ēvaṁ pā0 kā0 ॥

' hā putta ! āgaēṇa vi kīsa taē gōviō mahaṁ appā ? । duhasāyarammi paḍiō kiṁvā vi uvēkkhiō bahuyaṁ ? ॥413 ॥1445 ॥

taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā mucchāvihalaṁghalō dharāpīḍhē । paḍiō taṁ daṭṭaṇaṁ lōgō vi hu dukkhaō jāō || 444 || 1476 ॥
vāyāīdāṇēṇa ya satthīhūō khaṇēṇa naraṇāhō । tō dhaṇaēṇaṁ bhaṇiō 'avalaṁbasu dhīrayaṁ nāha ! || 445 || 1477॥
satthīkarēmi kumaraṁ khaṇamēttēṇaṁ ṇa ēttha saṁdēhō । siricakkēsari bhayavaividinnarayaṇa ppabhāvēṇa' ||446 ॥1478॥
pakkhāliūṇa ya taō rayaṇaṁ sittō jalēṇa nivataṇaō । suttō iva ṇiddakhaē samuṭṭhiō tō viyaṁbhaṁtō ॥447 ॥ 79 ॥
puṭṭhō ya naravarēṇaṁ 'kiṁ bāhai kiṁci ēttha tuha dēhē ' ! sō bhaṇai 'tāya ! na hu kiṁci bāhaē maha sarīrammi' ॥ 448 ॥ 1480 ॥
tō harisabharāvunnō āisai ṇivō 'karēha rē ! sigdhaṁ । maha suyajammē vva daḍhaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ mahārammaṁ ॥449॥1481॥
tēhiṁ vi 'taha tti' vihiyaṁ nivō vi sammāṇiūṇa tō dhaṇayaṁ । harisabharaṇibbharaṁgō vaccai ṇiyayammi bhavaṇammi ||450॥1482 ॥
aha annamma diṇammi mēlittā savvabaṁdhavē sēṭṭhī । gaṁtūṇa ṇivasamīvē bhaṇai suyaṁ 'putta ! sāha || 451 ॥ 1483 ॥
amhāṇubarōhēṇaṁ viṇiggaēṇaṁ iō taē taiyā । jaṁ kiṁci samaṇubhūyaṁ suhaṁ va dukkhaṁ va ṇissēsa' ||452 ॥ 1484 ॥
tō bhai imō 'jai tāya ! kōuyaṁ suṇaha ēgacittēṇaṁ । jaha tumbhēhiṁ bhiḍiō viṇiggaō jaha ya gēhāō || 453 ॥ 1485 ॥
jaha saravarammi pattō, jaha viddhō, jaha ya pakkhiṇā nīō। jaha pāḍiyaṁ suvaṇṇaṁ, rayaṇāī jaha ya gahiyāī ॥ 454 ॥ 1486 ॥

jaha diṭṭhā varakannā, tavyayaṇēṇaṁ jahā hai ō rakkhō । jaha pariṇīyā kannā, jaha pattō puṇa vi kūbammi ॥ 456 ॥ 1488 ॥

sōūṇaṁ sūrō jaṁpaṛa kara kōrayaṁ vihēūṇa । 'amhāṇa'ṇuggahō cciya ēsō accaṁta aigaruō ॥ 488 || 1520॥
jaṁ kannā karaṇaṁ aṇuggahaṁ kuṇai amha bhō ! dēvō । tā kumarasaṁtiya ciya kannā ēsā hu, kē amhē ? ' ॥489॥1521॥

jai tassa mamaṁ dāhiha, tō haṁ appāṇayaṁ vivāissaṁ' । taṁ sōūṇaṁ sūrō jāō sūrō vva gahagahiō ॥ 491 ॥1523॥
pabhaṇai ya 'maṁti ! kajaṁ ēyaṁ ēvaṁvihaṁ ihaṁ tāva । tā vaccaha niyāṇē ahayaṁ tu imaṁ aṇuṇaēmi' ॥ 492 ॥ 1524 ॥
tō vimaṇa-dummaṇamaṇō maṁtī vi hu kahai naravariṁdassa । taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā vajrēṇa haō vya saṁjāō ॥ 493 ।। 1525 ॥
sūrō vi hu taṁ kannaṁ bhayabhīō ṇaravarassa aṇuṇēi । taha vi na sā paḍivajjai, jaṁpai taṁ caiva puvyuttaṁ ॥ 494 ॥1526॥
tō sūrēṇaṁ gaṁtuṁ tavvayaṇaṁ akkhiyaṁ ṇariṁdassa । rāyā vi hu gaṁtūṇaṁ sāhai kumarassa ṇīsēsaṁ ॥495 ॥1527 ॥
kumarō vi tayaṁ sōuṁ kāmāvatthāē bāulīhūō । ētyaṁtarammi pattō dhaṇaō rāyassa pāsamma ॥ 496 ॥1528 ॥
jaṁpai ya 'aja tubbhē kiṁ dīsaha aisaēṇa āuliyā ? ' । rāyā vi bhaṇai 'puttaya ! kiṁ karimō tujjha lahubhāyā ॥ 497॥1529॥ 10
dūraṁ kāmāvatthāē ṇivaḍiō muṇai nēya sō kiṁ pi । pāṇāṇa vi saṁdēhē, vaṭṭai kannā vi niravēkkhā ॥ 498 ॥ 1530॥

1
tō amhāṇa vi puttaya ! mannējjasu ēttha jīyasaṁdēha' । taṁ sōūṇaṁ dhaṇaō jaṁpai karakōrayaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 499॥1531॥
'ētthaṁ pi dēva ! rayaṇaṁ vijai cakkēsarī maha dinaṁ । tā tassa pahāvēṇaṁ sāhēmi imaṁ pi lahu kajaṁ' ||500॥1532॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā harisiyacittō papaī 'vaccha ! | kuṇasu payattaṁ sigghaṁ, mā sē accāhiyaṁ hōhī' || 501 ॥1533॥
tō āṇēuṁ rayaṇaṁ mēllai kumarassa sannigāsammi । bhaṇiō ya 'imaṁ pūyasu jēṇa lahu sijjhaē kañjaṁ ॥ 502 ॥ 1534॥
kumarō vi hu kaṁḍaggayapāṇō vi samuṭṭhiūṇa kicchēṇa । pūēi tayaṁ rayaṇaṁ tō jaṁ jāyaṁ tayaṁ suṇaha ॥ 503 ॥ 1535 ॥
sahasa tti sā kumārī mannē jammaṁtaraṁ va pallaṭṭā । jaṁpai sahīē puraō 'nisuṇasu sahi ! majjha buttaṁtaṁ ॥ 504 ॥ 1536॥
ēttiyavēlaṁ ahayaṁ kumāranāmaṁ pi nēya visahatī । saṁpai sahi ! acchariyaṁ baṭṭai maha māṇasē garuyaṁ ||505 || 1537॥

jamhā mannāmi ahaṁ jai kumarō sigghu hōi maha bhattā । tāṁ hōi jīviyaṁ maha, aha navi tō jaṁti maha pāṇā' ॥ 506 ॥1538 ॥
tō taṁ sōūṇa sahī sigdhaṁ gaṁtuṁ kahēi jaṇayassa । jaha 'sā tumha kumārī kumaramaī aja saṁjāyā' ॥ 507 ।। 1539 ॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ sūrō harisabharēṇaṁ na māi aṁgammi । gaṁtuṁ nivassa pāsē sāhai savvaṁ jahāvattaṁ ॥ 508 || 1540 ॥
rāyā vi hu tōsavasā kumarassa kahāvaē tayaṁ savvaṁ । sōūṇa imō vi daḍhaṁ jāō amaēṇa sittō vva ॥ 509॥1541॥

rāyā vi kālaharaṇassa bhīruō saddiūṇa jōisiyaṁ । pucchai vivāhalaggaṁ tēṇa vi gaṇiūṇa kahiyamiṇaṁ ॥ 510 ।। 1542 ॥
jaha 'dēva ! pabhāyammiṁ kumarī - kumarāṇa sōhaṇaṁ laggaṁ' । rāyā vi tayaṁ sōuṁ jhaḍatti kārēi sāmaggiṁ ॥ 511 ॥1543 ॥
tō biiyammi diṇammiṁ pariṇīyā tēṇa sā vibhūīē । bhuṁjai pamuiyacittō tīē samaṁ uttamē bhōē || 512 || 1544 ॥
ēvaṁ acchaṁtāṇaṁ annadiṇē jhatti naravariṁdassa । jāyā sirammi viyaṇā uppannaṁ dāruṇaṁ sūlaṁ ॥ 513 | 1545॥
jāō ya dāhajaraō tēhiṁ taō pīḍiō daḍhaṁ ēsō । vējakiriyāē rōgō uvasamai na thōmēttaṁ pi ॥ 514 || 1546 ॥
taha maṁta-taṁta jaṁtāiēhiṁ vihiēhiṁ bahupayārēhiṁ । uvayārēhiṁ kahiṁcivi ubasamai na rāiṇō pīḍā ॥515॥1547 ॥
ēvaṁ vaṭṭaṁtammi āuliō takkhaṇēṇa ṇivalōgō । sōūṇa imaṁ dhaṇaō samāgaō rāyapāsamma || 516 || 1548 ॥
ghēttūṇa tayaṁ rayaṇaṁ rōyaharaṁ cakkiṇīē jaṁ dinnaṁ । pucchai ya 'dēva ! sāhaha, kā pīḍā tumha dēhammi ? ' ॥ 517॥1549॥
avalaṁbiūṇa sattaṁ jaṁpai rāyā vi 'vaccha ! maha dēhē । jā vaṭṭai kira pīḍā sā sattūṇaṁ pi mā hōu || 518 ।। 1550 ।।
vacchaya ! jāṇāmi ahaṁ niggacchahiṁ ēva tāva maha pāṇā ? ' । taṁ sōuṁ dhaṇaēṇa vi ōhaliyaṁ taṁ mahārayaṇaṁ ।।519 ॥1551 ॥
bhaṇiō ya 'piyaha ēyaṁ dēva ! jalaṁ, jēṇa uvasamai pīḍā' । pīē ya tammi rāyā mukkō ṇīsēsarōgēhiṁ ॥ 520॥1552॥
1. tīya tru0 | 2. vamittaṁ kā0 ॥

taṁ acca bhuyacariyaṁ daṭuṁ dhaṇayassa vimhiō rāyā । ciṁtai "na ēyatullō annō puhaīyalē atthi ॥ 521 ॥ 1553 ॥
gurupuṇṇapabhāvēṇa jāyā maha ēiṇā samaṁ pīī । ēsō ya ēttha ēgō maha suya maha pāṇadāya ti ॥ 522|| 1554॥
sappurisacēṭṭhiyāṇaṁ mōllaṁ na hu atthi jīvalōgammi । jamhā supurisacēṭṭhā labbhai na hu davyasaṁkhāē ॥ 523॥1555॥
kō kuṇau tāṇa mōllaṁ supurisarayaṇāṇa ēttha puhaīē। jāṇa maṇē saṁkappō parakajjaṁ cēva niyakajjaṁ ।। 524 ।। 1556॥
jē niyakajjaṁ mōttuṁ kuṇaṁti parakajjamēva aṇudiyahaṁ । kiraṁ supurisāṇa tāṇaṁ kō ṇu samō hōu puhavīē ? ॥ 525 ॥ 1557॥
bhuvaṇaṁ pi bhūsiyamiṇaṁ sappurisēhiṁ na ēttha saṁdēhō । tēhiṁ ciya supavittaṁ vihiyaṁ, kiṁ vā viyappēṇa ? " ॥ 526 ॥ 1558 ।।
iya ciṁtiūṇa rāyā niyayasuyāō vi pēcchaē ahiyaṁ । jaṁ kira kiṁcivi kajjuṁ kuṇai tayaṁ pucchiuṁ dhaṇayaṁ ॥ 527॥1559॥
paṁcamarayaṇassa puṇō māhappaṁ tēsu tēsu ḍāṇēsu । savvattha cēva payaḍaṁ puvvōiyajhagaḍayāīsu ॥ 528 ॥ 1560 ॥
jaṁ dūravihaḍiyā vihu lacchī dhaṇayassa puṇa vi saṁghaḍiyā । taṁ payaḍaṁ māhappaṁ lacchīnilayassa rayaṇassa ॥ 529 ॥ 1561॥
jaṁ ca maṇavaṁchiyāṇaṁ samatthavatthūṇa hōi saṁpattī । dhaṇayassa taṁ pi jāṇasu māhappaṁ lacchinilayassa ॥530|| 1562 ॥
ēvaṁ jāva bahukālō vōlīṇō tāva puravarē tammi । viharaṁtō saṁpattō sūrī sīlaṁdharō ṇāma ||531|| 1563॥

cauvihanāṇasamaggō, vararuvēṇaṁ aṇaṁgasāricchō । khaṁtīē dharaṇisamō, gaṁbhīratēṇa jalahi vva ॥ 532॥ 1564 ॥
caṁdō vva sōmayāē, tavatēēṇaṁ divāyarō cēva । sajalajalaō sarēṇaṁ, dhammō ruvi vva paccakkhō || 533 ॥ 1565 ॥
tassa ya vaṁdaṇahēuṁ nīsaraī sayalapuravarajaṇōhō । hāō kayabalikammō siyavatthāharaṇasōhillō ॥ 534 ॥ 1566 ॥
dhaṇaō viha niyabhavaṇē uvariṁ caḍiō kahiṁ pi pēcchēi । taṁ vaccaṁta lōyaṁ pucchai niyayaṁ parīvāraṁ ॥ 535 ॥ 1567 ॥
'kattha imō jāi jaṇō saṁvvō vi hu pūyapaḍalayavihatthō ? ' । aha jāṇiyaparamatthō sāhai ēgō tahiṁ purisō ॥ 536 ॥ 1568 ।। 5
'sāmi ! iha kō vi nāṇī samāgaō muṇiyasayalasatthatthō । ujjāṇē tassa imō jāi jaṇō vaṁdaṇanimittaṁ' ॥537 ॥ 1569॥
bhaṇai dhaṇō 'jai ēvaṁ, tō sajjaṁ rahavaraṁ karēha tti । jēṇa'mhē vi vayāmō tassa muṇiṁdassa namaṇatthaṁ' ॥ 538 ॥1570॥
tēhiṁ vi 'tahatti' vihiē tō rahavaramāruhittu jāi dhaṇō । vaṁdittu pāyakamalaṁ muṇivaiṇō visai tappuraō ॥ 539 ।। 1571 ॥
bhayavaṁ pi hu patthāvai dhammuvaēsaṁ dhaṇāiparisāē । jaha nisuṇaha 'bhō bhavvā ! maha vayaṇaṁ avahiyā hōuṁ ॥ 540॥1572 ॥

aha bhāvēṇa kalaṁkai taṁ dhammaṁ aṁtaraṁtarā jīvō। tō duhavimissiyāī lahai suhāī jahā mahaṇō” || 3 || 1575 ।।
kayakarayalaṁjaliuḍō kairaruhapariṇitakiraṇaniyarēṇa । kabburiyasirōruhabhārabhūsiō bhaṇai dhaṇanāmō ॥4॥1576 ॥
'bhayavaṁ ! kō sō mahaṇō ? kaha vā tēṇaṁ kalaṁkiō dhammō ? । kaha vā duhamissāiṁ suhāī tēṇēha pattāī ? ' ॥ 5 ॥ 1577॥
aha sajalajalaharōralligahiraṇigghōsapūriyadiyaṁtō । bhayavaṁ dhaṇēṇa puṭṭhō ēvaṁ kahiuṁ samādattō ॥ 6 ॥1578 ॥
"atthēttha bharahavāsē rayaṇapuraṁ nāma puravaraṁ rammaṁ । bahuvihavakaliya - jaṇaniyarasaṁkulaṁ tiyasanayaraṁ va ॥ 1 ॥1579 ॥
taṁ parivālai rāyā aṇēyasāmaṁtapaṇayapayakamalō । uttattakaṇayavaṇṇō kaṇayarahō ṇāma supasiddhō ॥ 2 ॥1580 ॥
tassa'tthi ra saricchā dēvī kaṇayappaha tti supasiddhā । sayalaṁtēurasārā guṇagaṇajuttā kalākaliyā ॥3॥1581॥
tīē samaṁ varabhōē bhuṁjaṁtō kulakamāgayaṁ rajjaṁ । nīīē paripālai māṇitō buṁhajaṇēṇaṁ ॥4 ॥1582 ॥
ēttō ya tammi nayarē sēṭṭhī parivasai nāma vasudattō । paṇaiyaṇapūriyāsō gōravvō naravariṁdassa ॥5॥1583 ॥
tassa ya guṇagaṇakaliyā vasuṁdharī nāma atthi varapattī । tāṇaṁ ca suō mahaṇō uppannō guṇakalākaliō || 6 || 1584 ॥
nāūṇa jōvvaṇatthaṁ samāṇakula- rūva - jōvvaṇaguṇaḍuḍaṁ । sōmasiriṁ nāmēṇaṁ jaṇaēhiṁ vivāhiō kannaṁ ||7|| 1585 ॥

sō tīē samaṁ bhōē bhatta'ṇurattāē bhuṁjai jahicchaṁ । na viyāṇēi gayaṁ pi hu kālaṁ dēvō vya niccitō ॥ 8 ॥1586 ॥
annamma diṇammi imō āruhiuṁ rahavarammi tuṁgammi । ujjāṇiyānimittaṁ ujjāṇē vaccai samittō ॥ 9 ॥1587 ।।
tattha vi pavarapaēsē vitthiṇṇō maṁḍavō viṇimmaviō । ullōyabhatticittō vimukkavarakusumaōūlō ||10|| 1588 ।।
tattha ya bhōjaṁ khajjaṁ lējjha pēyaṁ cauvvihāhāraṁ । bhuṁjai saha mittēhiṁ āyamai taō kamēṇa sō ॥11॥1589 ॥
gihittu paṁcasōgaṁdhiyaṁ tu muhavāsayaṁ sutaṁbōlaṁ । pēcchittu khaṇaṁ ēgaṁ pēcchaṇayaṁ lōyaṇāṇaṁdaṁ ॥ 12 ॥ 1590 ।।
uṭṭittu taō mittēhiṁ saṁjuō pēcchaē varujjāṇaṁ । bahupāyavasaṁkiṇṇaṁ phulla-pphalariddhisusamiddhaṁ ॥ 13 ॥ 1591॥
aha ēkkammi paēsē suvivittē phāsuē maṇabhirāmē । tasa - thāvarajīvēhiṁ vivajjiē sāhujaṇajōgē ॥ 14 ॥ 1592 ॥
uttattakaṇayavaṇṇaṁ tiyasaṁ piva rūvasaṁpayasamēyaṁ । paḍhamavaē baṭṭaṁta caṁdō iva sōmayākaliyaṁ ||15|| 1593 ॥
khaṁtī-muttipahāṇaṁ tavatēyasirīē suṭu dippataṁ । rattāsōyatalammi suniviṭṭaṁ jhāṇagayacittaṁ ॥ 16॥1594॥
pēcchai ya varamuṇi sō daṭṭu ruvāiēhiṁ vimhaiō । pucchai niyaē mittē 'kō ēsō ?' kahaha maha purisō ||17|| 1595 ॥
mittēhiṁ taō bhaṇiyaṁ 'ēsa muṇī savvasaṁgaparimukkō । ēgatammi mahappā dhammajjhāṇaṁ jhiyāēi ||18|| 1596 ।।

tō sēṭṭhiputta ! gaṁtuṁ vaṁdasu ēyaṁ payāhiṇaṁ kāuṁ । varabhattisaṁpauttō appāṇaṁ kuṇasu supavittaṁ ॥ 19 ॥ 1597॥
jēṇēvaṁvihavaramuṇijaṇāṇa pāyāṇa vaṁdaṇēṇā'vi । pāvakhaēṇaṁ pāṇī sujjhai iya bhannai viūhiṁ' ॥ 20 ॥ 1598 ॥
'ēva bhavau 'tti mahaṇō vaṁdai pāē muṇissa gaṁtūṇa । sāhū vi jhāṇajōgaṁ ubasaṁharijaṁ taō bhaṇai ॥ 21 ॥ 1599 ॥
“nīsēsaduriyadalaṇō sāsayasivaṇayaramaggarahapavarō । tuha hōu dhammalābhō kammamahākarighaḍāsīhō" ॥22॥1600 ॥
dinnē ya dhammalābhē mahaṇō uvavisai tassa payamūlē । sāhū bi tassa bhāvaṁ nāuṁ patthāvaē dhammaṁ ||23|| 1601 ॥
“bhō bhavyā ! dukkharukkhē bhavasayagahaṇē kōvadāvāṇalillē, māyāvaṁsīkuḍaṁgē kalilabharamahāsāvayāiṇṇamajjhē ।
māṇaddīruddarūvē maraṇakarivarē lōhakhaḍḍāvihaḍḍē, duvvāruggappamāyappasaragiriṇaīduggamaggappayārē ॥ 1॥1602 ॥
vāhīvēyālabhīmē jarapasaramahārakkhasīsaṁpauttē, dāridduddāmavagdhē bhayajaṇayamahāmōha kaṁḍīravālē ।
saṁsārāsāraraṇṇē sivapuragamaṇaṭuāṇamūḍhāṇa ṇicaṁ, pāṇīṇaṁ satthavāhō bhavai ya dulahō dēsaē jō sumaggaṁ || 2 || 1603 ॥
laḍhūṇaṁ māṇusattaṁ aisayadulahaṁ cōllayāīhiṁ lōē, didrutēhiṁ dēsēhiṁ muṇigaṇavaiṇā bhāsiēhiṁ varēhiṁ ।
tēṇāiṭummi dhammē sivasuhajaṇaṇē ujjamō paṁḍiēṇaṁ, kāyavyō hōi jamhā kuṇaha ya vimalaṁ taṁ bhavaṁtō vi ṇicaṁ " ॥3॥1604॥

tō bhai muṇī 'bhaddaya ! pālēhi mahavvayāī paṁcēva । rāībhōyaṇaviraīchuṭṭāī tiguttiguttāiṁ ॥4॥1606 ॥
paṁcasu samiīsu tahā samiyāī rāga - dōsavihuyāī । khaṁtāisamēyāī paḍivajiya bhāvajailiṁgaṁ' ॥5॥1607॥

jaha jaha sā ṇipphajjai pēcchai ya maṇōharaṁ taha tahēva । rasavattāisaēṇaṁ vaēi apparimiyaṁ puṇa vi ॥ 15॥1617॥
kārāvēi paiṭuṁ varavicchaḍēṇa bhāvaṇākaliō । ghōsāvēi amāriṁ dēi ya saṁghassa varadāṇaṁ ॥ 16 ॥1618 ॥
kārāvaē ya aṭṭhāhiyāipūyaṁ maṇōbhirāmillaṁ । sāhammiyapaḍivattiṁ karēi taṁbōlamāīhiṁ ॥17॥1619॥
ēvaṁ savvaṁ kāuṁ ciṁtai " vaiyaṁ maē bahuṁ davvaṁ । hōhī phalaṁ na vatti ya kō kira ēyaṁ viyāṇēi ? ॥ 18 ॥ 1620 ॥
satthē puṇō bhanna jaha hōi aṇōvamaṁ phalaṁ ēttha । maha buddhī saṁsaiyā na hu ḍāi viṇicchaē kahavi " ॥19॥1621 ॥
iya saṁsayajuttō vi hu karēi pūyāiyaṁ asēsaṁ pi । aha annammi diṇammiṁ jā ciṭui gēhamajjhatthō ||20|| 1622 ॥
tā tabasōsiyadēhē iriyāsamiē subaṁbhacēṁcaiē । viharaṇahēuṁ ēṁtē pēcchai barasāhuṇō dōnni ॥21॥1623॥
tē daṭuṇubhijirarōmaṁcō niyai rasavaī sahasā । bahubhakkhāisamēyaṁ pēcchēuṁ taṁ samūsasiō ॥22॥1624 ॥
paḍilāi tē muṇiṇō bhattimbharaṇibbharō sahatthēhiṁ । vaṁdittu tō visāi ciṁtai ya taō " ahaṁ dhannō ॥ 23॥1625॥

pacchāhuttagāmī aṁbaracāī ya । jō ya rāyā sukaṁtō sōmō ya, paraṁ na mayalaṁchaṇō sasakō ya । jō ya acalō
vaṇarāivibhūsiō sukaḍaō ya, paraṁ na duṭṭusattāhiṭṭiō agaō yatti । avi ya-
jō dēvō vva surūvō, maimāhappēṇa suragurusamāṇō । parauvayārammi sibī, cāēṇaṁ cakkabaṭṭi vya ॥ 4 ॥1694 ॥
tassa ya rāiṇō saṁti savrvvatēurappahāṇāō vasuṁdhara - aṇudharināmāō dōnni mahādēvīō, jāō ya-
mahāḍavīō vya sumayaṇāō subāhāō ya, mahākaivāṇīō thva suvaṇṇāō suviyaḍūḍhāō ya, mahāṇaīō vyaṁ 5
supaōharāō suramaṇāō yatti । kiṁca-
piyabhāṇirīō suhayāō rūvakaliyāō dhammanirayāō। sukalāō sunāṇāō niyapaibhattāō rattāōṁ ॥5॥1695 ॥
tāhiṁ ca samaṁ visayasuhamaṇuhavaṁtassa naravaiṇō vaccaē kālō ।

divvaṁ bhōgalacchimaṇuhaviūṇa cuō samrāṇō samuppannō vasuṁdharīē gabbhē । tasmi va gatyē pēcchai sā cattāri 1
mahāsumiṇē । tē ya daṭṭuṇa jaṁbhāyamāṇavayaṇā harisabasavisappamāṇahiyayā vibuddhā dēbī ciṁtaē- "hēta ! maē ēgasamaēṇa
cēva cattāri mahāsumiṇagā diṭṭhā, tā sāhēmi imē daibassa, " tti ciṁtiūṇa samuṭṭhiyā sayaṇīyāō, rāyahaṁsiyāsari-
siyāē gaīē gayā ramaṇasamīvē, uṭuviō rāyā kōmalavayaṇēhiṁ, abbhaṇunnāyā ya tēṇa niviṭṭhā maṇikaṇagara-

yaṇanimmiyammi pavarabhāsaṇammi, 'jaya jaya' saddapurassaraṁ ca kamalamaulasarisaṁ karayalaṁjaliṁ sīsē kāūṇa vinnaviu-
māḍhattā, avi ya-
'dēva ! ahaṁ sayaṇi ramaṇijē suhapasuttayā ajja । saṁkhadalavimalasarisaṁ caudasaṇaṁ gattasuvibhattaṁ ॥ 6 ॥1696 ॥
mayagaṁdhaluddhaphullaṁdhuēhiṁ ruṇuruṇiyagaṁḍapavibhāyaṁ । vayaṇammiṁ pavisaṁta pēcchāmi mahāgayaṁ paḍhamaṁ ||7|| 1697 ॥
bīyaṁ ca thōrakhadhaṁ ḍhēkkataṁ caṁdakiraṇasamavaṇṇaṁ । pīṇataṇuṁ suvisālaṁ varavasabhaṁ savvaguṇajuttaṁ ॥ 8॥1698 ॥
taiyaṁ ca kalākaliyaṁ sucaṁdimāpasaradhavaliyadiyaṁta । ānaṁdiyasayalajaṇaṁ pēcchāmi mahōsahīnāhaṁ ॥ 9 ॥1699 ॥
pēcchāmi taha cautthaṁ kuvalaya sayavattarēṇupiṁjariyaṁ । aisacchanīrapuṇṇaṁ sarōvaraṁ pālitaruniyaraṁ ॥ 10 ॥ 1700॥
tā nāha ! tāṇa majjha sāhasu sumiṇāṇa kiṁ phalaṁ hōhī ? ' । rāyā vi haṭu-tuṭṭō taṁ sōuṁ māi nō dēhē ॥11॥1701॥
bhai ya pahigmaṇasō 'dēvi ! taē uttamā imē diṭṭhā | sumiṇā savvapahāṇā tā puttō hōhiī tujjha ॥12॥1702॥
puhaīyalappahāṇō namaṁtanaranāhapaṇayapayakamalō' । ' ēvaṁ ti hōu' dēvī sumiṇē sammaṁ paḍicchēi ||13|| 1703 ॥
gaṁtūṇaya niyaṭhāṇē sā sammaṁ pālaē niyaṁ garbha । rāyā vi sumiṇapāḍhagamāpucchai vihiyapaḍivattī ||14|| 1704 ॥
pabhaṇai ēsō 'naravara ! balabhaddō tujjha hōhiī puttō' । taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā akkhaṛa dēvīē savvaṁ pi || 15 || 1705।।

ēvaṁ ca sōūṇa haṭutuṭṭā ganbhapōsaṇēhiṁ pōsaṁtī taṁ gandhaṁ suhaṁsuhēṇaṁ parivaes | pasūyā niyakālakkamēṇaṁ

' vaddhāvijjasi naravara ! aṇannasarisēṇa pīinivahēṇa । dēvī vasuṁdhara jaō ajja pasūyā varaṁ puttaṁ ' ॥ 16 ॥ 1706 ॥
1
taṁ ca sōūṇa paharisabasakhalaṁtavayaṇēṇaṁ dāūṇa pāritōsigaṁ dāsacēḍīē kārāviyaṁ mahābadbhāvaṇayaṁ । kamēṇa ya saṁpattē
bārasamadiṇē kayaṁ kumārassa ṇāmadhējjaṁ aparājiō tti । girikaṁdarasamallīṇō vba caṁpagapāyavō baḍūḍhaē dēhōvacaēṇaṁ ti ।
annayā kayāi aṇuṁdharī vi jāyā āvannasattā । suhapasuttā ya rayaṇīē carimajāmē pēcchai satta mahāsumiṇāṇi,
avi ya-
'kuṁdaṁḍaka - phalihavannaṁ thiralaṭupauṭukuḍiladāḍhālaṁ । rāmaṁ līlāyaṁtaṁ sā pēcchai mayavaī paḍhamaṁ ||17|| 1707 ॥
paumāsaṇōvavituṁ vaṇakarikarakīramāṇaabhisēyaṁ । dvōyahinīrēṇa bīyaṁ tu niyacchaē lacchiṁ ||18|| 1708 ॥
paumāvabōhaṇakaraṁ ninnāsiyasayalatimirasaṁghāyaṁ । yaḍiyapayatthasatthaṁ taiyaṁ puṇa pēcchaē sūraṁ ॥ 19॥1709॥
sacchayaranīrapuṇṇaṁ varakusumōmāliyaṁ kaṇayaghaḍiyaṁ puṁḍariyamuhapihāṇaṁ cautthayaṁ pēcchaē kuṁbhaṁ ||20|| 1710॥
bahurayaṇacittiyatalaṁ kallōlābattarēhirataraṁgaṁ । jalyarasayasaṁkinnaṁ avalōyai paṁcamaṁ jalahiṁ ॥ 21॥ 1711॥

bahuvannarayaṇakiriṇōhapasarasaṁjāyasakkakōyāṁḍaṁ । chṭuṁ pēcchai dēvī rayaṇāṇa samuccayaṁ tuṁgaṁ ॥ 22 ॥ 1712 ॥

sattaṇhaṁ mahāsumiṇāṇaṁ phalaṁ ?' ti । tēṇā'vi avadhāriūṇa sammaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, jahā - 'mahārāya ! paḍhamō puttō baladēvō, imō
ya bīyaputtō vāsudēvō bhavissai' । taṁ pi nivēiyaṁ rāiṇā aṇudharidēvīē । sā vi paramāṇaṁdasuhamaṇuhavaṁtī niyayasamaē
pasūyā sihigala - gavala - guliya-tālā - 'livalayavannaṁ dārayaṁ ti । tattha vi kayaṁ baddhāvaṇayaṁ nivyattē ya bārasamadiṇē

rūvāisayasaṁpannā navajōvvaṇaṁ ti । vivāhiyā ya samāṇakula- rūba- jōbbaṇaguṇāō bāliyāō ।

caṁdaṇa - yaṁdaṇa-ēlā- lavaṁga- kakkōla - nāga sāgēhiṁ । pūgā 'garu-tagarēhiṁ rēhai taṁ naṁdaṇavaṇaṁ va ॥ 1 ॥1714 ॥
1
tattha ya jā khaṇamēgaṁ vīsamaṁḍa asōgataruvaratalammi । tā diṭṭō tēṇa muṇī jhāṇatyō ṇiccalasarīrō ॥2॥ 1715 ॥
taṁ daddūṇaṁ rāyā bhattivasullasiyabahalarōmaṁcō । tipayāhiṇaṁ vihēuṁ vaṁdai paramēṇa viṇaṇa || 3 || 1716॥ avi ya-
'paṁcamahavyayadhāraya ! khaṁtāidasappayāraguṇakaliya ! | dukkaratavasusiyaṁgaya ! tujjha namō hōu muṇivasaha !' ॥ 4 ॥ 1917 ॥
ēvaṁ ca nisāmiūṇa muṇiṇā vi jhāṇajōgamuvasaṁhariūṇa dinnō rāiṇō dhammalābhō, avi ya-
"narayapura'ggalasarisō sivapura ararīnivāḍaṇa kuṭhārō । tuha hōu dhammalābhō pahāṇa kappahumasaricchō" ॥1॥1718 ।।
ladvāsīsō ya ṇisaṇṇō muṇiṇō ṇa'ccāsapaṇē ṇariṁdō suddhabhūmīē, bhaṇiyaṁ ca bhayavayā, avi ya-
“saṁsārassa u mūlaṁ kōhāīyā u sōlasa kasāyā । jāṇa vasagō maṇussō bhamai mahābhavakaḍillammi || 1 || 1719॥
tā bhō bhavvā ! ēē parihariyabbā narēṇa buddhimayā । nāūṇa tassarūvaṁ jiṇavaradhammammi jaṁ diṭṭu " || 2 || 1720 ॥
imaṁ ca bhayavaō muhāraviṁdaviṇiggayaṁ vayaṇamāyanniūṇa lalāḍataḍabaddhaghaḍiyakarayalaṁjaliuḍēṇa viṇṇattaṁ rāiṇā,
jahā - ' bhayavaṁ ! kē imē sōlasa kasāyā ? ' । bhayavayā bhaṇiyaṁ - 'suṇasu mahārāya !'
"kōhō māṇō māyā lōbhō caurō ya hōṁti caubhēyā । aṇaṁta apaccakkhāṇā paccakkhāṇā ya saṁjalaṇā || 3 || 1721॥

ē
tattha ya kōvō paḍhamō muṇasu aṇatāṇubaṁdhiō rāya ! । pavvayarāisamāṇō dāruṇaduhadāyagō pāvō ||4|| 1722॥
puḍhavīrāisamāṇō appacakkhāṇanāmaō bīō । taiō paccakkhāṇō dhūlīrēhāsamō rāya ! ॥5॥1723 ॥
saṁjalaṇō yē cautthō pāṇiyarēhāsamō viyāṇāhi । māṇāiṇō vi ēvaṁ caubbihā hōṁti vinēyā ||6||1724॥
sēlatthaṁbha-'ṭṭhiya-kaṭu-tiṇisalayasarisaō bhavē māṇō । vaṁsī ya miṁṭasiṁga gōmuttuvalēhaṇī māyā || 7 || 1725॥
kimirāya-kaddamaṁjaṇa-haliddarāyappahaṁ muṇasu lōhaṁ । ēēsiṁ jē paḍhamā tē jāvajīviyā hōṁti ||8|| 1726॥
bīyā uṇa vārasiyā, taiyā caumāsiyā muṇēyavvā । pakkhaṭṭiī cautthā, ṇarayāigaīṇa tē hēū ॥ 9 ॥1727॥
ēvaṁ tē parikahiyā sōlasa vi ṇariṁda ! jāṇasu kasāyā । guruāvēsēṇa kayā bahubhavaduhadāiṇō hōṁti ॥10॥1728॥
āvēsēṇa viṇā uṇa thōyabhavē dēṁti dāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ । tamhā naravara ! appē vi mā kasāē karējāhi ॥ 11 ॥1729 ।
jamhā thēvassa vi dukkaḍassa garuyaṁ phalaṁ jiṇidēhiṁ । ṇiddiddhaṁ samayammiṁ jaha mittāṇaṁda māīṇaṁ ॥ 12 ॥ 1730॥
bhai niṁvō 'kē ēē mittāṇaṁdāiṇō viṇiddiṭṭhā ? | sāhēhi kōuyaṁ mē thēvammi vidukkaḍaphalammi' ॥13॥1731॥
bhaṇai muṇī 'jai cōjaṁ naravara ! tō suṇasu ēgacittēṇaṁ' । rāyā vi jōḍiyakarō jaṁpara 'sajjō ahaṁ sāmi !' ||14|| 1732 ॥
tō daṁtakiriṇavicchuriyanahayalō khuhiyajalahinigghōsō । aha akkhiuṁ payattō bhayavaṁ rāyāibōhatthaṁ || 15 | 1733॥

" asthi iha jaṁbuddīvē dīvē varabhārahammi vāsammi । nayaraguṇāṇa nihāṇaṁ suratilayaṁ nāma varanayaraṁ ||1|| 1734॥
jaṁ ca susālaṁ suramaṁdarō vva, bahusaṁvaraṁ varamuṇi vya । sarayanisa vva sutāraṁ susāvayaṁ aḍavikacchaṁ va ॥ 2 ॥ 1735 ॥
saggō vya sudēvaulaṁ, bahusaraṇaṁ sūranaravaikulaṁ va । saṁkhāṇaṁ va supayaī, viṇhu vva sudarisaṇādhāraṁ ||3|| 1736 ॥
kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ ? taṁ nayaraṁ sayalaguṇagaṇanihāṇaṁ । pālēi nīikaliō rāyā mayaraddhaō nāma || 4 || 1737॥
jō sūrō vva suvittō, bahuvāhō aḍavisēlaniyarō vya । ujjāṇaṁ piva sunaō, payapālō varuṇarāu vya ||5|| 1738 ॥
tassa'tthi mayaṇasēṇā sayalaṁtēurapahāṇayā dēvī । dhaṇulaṭṭī iva saguṇā, bahumēhā pāusasiri vva ॥6॥1739॥
sarayasirivva sukamalā, hēmaṁtasiri vva cārukayatilayā । sisirasiri vva suphaliṇī, vasaṁtalacchi vva kayamayaṇā ॥7॥1740 ॥
gimhasiri vva varēṇā, kiṁ bahuṇā ? sayalaguṇagaṇasamēyā । sā niyapaiṇā saddhiṁ bhuṁjai puṇṇa'jiē bhōē || 8 || 1741 ॥
aha annayā kayāī sayaṇi maharihē suhapasuttā। pēcchai pacchimajāmē paumasaraṁ viyasiyaṁ sumiṇē ॥ 9 ॥1742 ॥
taṁ pēcchiūṇa dēvī paḍibuddhā kahai niyayadaiyassa । tēṇa ya 'varasuyajammō' āiṭṭō hiducittēṇa ||10|| 1743 ॥
aha kamasō saṁpattē pasūisamayammi pasavaī dēvī । battīsalakkhaṇadharaṁ puttaṁ pasaraṁta kaṁtillaṁ ॥11॥ 1744 ॥

baddhāviō ya rāyā piyaṁgulaiyāē dāsacēḍīē । parituṭṭō naranāhō tīsē dāṇaṁ bahuṁ dāum̐ ||12|| 1745 ॥
baddhāvaṇayamahūsavamāisai samatthaṇiyayarajammi । rāyā'' ēsēṇa taō baddhāvaṇayaṁ kaha pavattaṁ ? || 13 || 1746 ॥
vajraē tūru aigahiraghaṇasaddayaṁ, naccaē pāulaṁ nihayadharaniddayaṁ ।
1
diē caḍulatō kkhāragurughaṭṭayaṁ, 'jaya-jayā' saddi āsīsaē bhaṭṭayaṁ || 14 || 1747॥
caṭṭasaṁghāu tappijjaē sāyaraṁ ēi gahiya'kkhayaṁ thījaṇaṁ nāyaraṁ ।
diē bhatta-pōttāiyaṁ dāṇayaṁ kijaē rāyalōyassa sammāṇayaṁ ||15|| 1748॥
iya kamasō vittammiṁ vaddhāvaṇayambhi uciyasamayammi । vihiyaṁ ca paumakēsaranāmaṁ sumiṇāṇusārēṇaṁ ॥ 16 ॥ 1749 ॥
aha vaḍūḍhaṁtō kamasō saṁpattō jāva aṭṭhamaṁ varisaṁ । tāva kalāyariēṇaṁ kalāō giṇhāviō sigghaṁ || 17 || 1750।।
pattō ya jōvvaṇammiṁ jā tā pariṇāviō naravarēṇaṁ । kannāō taō bhuṁjai juvarāyattē ṭhiō bhōē ||18|| 1751॥
aha annayā kayāī naranāhō niyayamattavāraṇaē । dēvīē samaṁ ciṭui kīlaṁtō vivihakīlāhiṁ ||19|| 1752 ॥
ciharē samārayaṁtī dēvī sasikiraṇanimmalaṁ ruiraṁ । paliyaṁ daṭṭu jaṁpai 'piyayama ! dūō samāyāō' ||20|| 1753 ॥
1. caṭula° jē0 kā0 ॥। 2. 'tōkkāragu' pā0 | 'tōkhāragu° jē0 ॥। 3. tuppi pā0 । tupi kā0 ॥

<pb n="197"/>

taṁ sōuṁ puhaibaī palōyaē tārataralanayaṇillō । jaṁpai kēlīē piyā 'kiṁ ubhaṁtō tumaṁ nāha ! ||21|| 1754 ॥
bahusamaraladdhavijaō vidūyamēttaṁ imaṁ giraṁ sōcā ? ' । bhaṇai nivō 'na hu bhaddē ! bhaēṇa taralāiō ahayaṁ ॥ 22 ॥1755 ॥
kiṁtu na pēcchāmi aō dūyaṁ, na ya sāhiō maha carēhiṁ । na ya paḍihārēṇa tahā, tumaṁ tu paribhāsasē ēvaṁ ॥ 23 ॥ 1756॥
na ya maha nayaṇēhiṁtō tujjha visēsēṇa nimmalā diṭṭhī । ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ vimhayataralō ahaṁ jāō' ||24|| 1757 ॥
bhāi taō sā dēvī 'dēva ! na amhāṇa ērisā tattī' । jaṁpai nivō vi ' tā kiṁ ēvaṁ maṁ vippayārēsi ? ' ॥ 25 ॥ 1758 ॥
sā bhai 'dēva ! kaiyā diṭṭhā haṁ aliyabhāsiṇī tumaē ? । kiṁtu tuha dhammadūō samāgaō paliyarūvēṇa' ॥ 26 ॥1759 ॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā ciṁtāvasamaulamāṇanayaṇajuō । ciṁtai " hā ! kaha ahayaṁ visayāmisakaddamē khuttō ॥ 27॥1760॥
thakkō ēttiyakālaṁ ? saṁpai buḍḍhattaṇammi kiṁ kāhaṁ ?" । aviyāṇiyanivabhāvā hasiūṇaṁ bhaṇai tō dēvī ||28|| 1761 ॥
'buḍḍhattaṇēṇa sāmiya ! jai lajjasi tō samatthanayarammi | paḍahayasaddēṇa phuḍaṁ ghōsāvissāmi ahamēva ' ॥ 29 ॥1762 ॥
" jō naraṇāhaṁ buḍḍhaṁ bhaṇihī sō sigdyamēva pāhuṇaō । pēsissihī niruttaṁ kīṇāsagharammi" tō rāyā ||30|| 1763 ॥
jaṁpai 'avivēīṇaṁ juttamiṇaṁ' jaṁpaē taō dēvī । 'jai ēvaṁ tō ciṁtābharēṇa kiṁ kāraṇaṁ gahiyā ?' ||31|| 1764 ॥
bhai niṁvō 'ciṁtāē bhaddē ! 'taṁ kāraṇaṁ nisāmēhiṁ । puvyapurisāṇucinnō aja maē laṁghiō maggō ||32|| 1765 ॥
1. nivō mē ciṁtā bhaddē jē0 || 2. kiṁ pā0 ॥
10
<pb n="198"/>

maha vaṁsē rāyāṇō adiṭupaliyā tavōvaṇē jaṁtā । puttē rajjē uviuṁ, bhōgāsattō ḍiō ahayaṁ ||33|| 1766 ॥
tā saṁpayaṁ pi rajjē ḍāvēuṁ paumakēsaraṁ dēvi ! । ārannagō pasatthō hōhāmi muṇī na saṁdēhō' ||34|| 1767॥
taṁ sōūṇaṁ dēvī bajrēṇa va tāḍiyā gayā mucchaṁ । vīsatthā puṇa jaṁpai 'hā sāmi ! kimērisaṁ bhaṇasi ? ||35|| 1768॥
ēsa kaō parihāsō, saccaṁ ciya taṁ puṇō ya maṁtēsi' । bhaṇai ṇivō 'hāsēṇa vi ghēppai jaṁ sōhaṇaṁ vayaṇaṁ ॥ 36 ॥1769॥
tā ēsa maē kahiō dēvi ! tuhaṁ nicchaō, na saṁdēhō । kallaṁ ciya ghēttavvaṁ maē vayaṁ tāvasāina' ||37|| 1770 ॥
bhaṇai imā 'jai sāmiya ! bhatta'ṇurattaṁ mamaṁ paricayasi । tō tumaē cciya saddhiṁ ahamavi kāhāmi tavamaulaṁ' ॥ 38 ॥ 1771 ॥
tō jaṁpai naranāhō 'juttamiṇaṁ dēvi ! tuha vivēyassa' । kumaraṁ pravēttu rajē saha tīē tāvasō jāō ||39|| 1772 ॥
jā paripālai kiriyaṁ sā dēvī tēṇa bhattuṇā samayaṁ । tā vaḍḍhiuṁ pavattō gabbhō jō puvyasaṁbhūō ||40|| 1773 ॥
taṁ pēcchiūṇa mayaraddhaēṇa puṭṭhā 'kimērisaṁ bhaddē ! | dīsai tujjha sarūyaṁ ?' sā jaṁpai 'suṇasu vinnatiṁ ॥ 41 ॥ 1774 ॥
puvvaṁ ciya saṁbhūō ganbhō maha āsi kiṁtu navi siṭṭhō । taiya ciya niyavaya aṁtarāya bhayabhīyahiyayāē ' ॥ 42 ॥ 1775 ॥
bhaṇai imō 'na hu juttaṁ vihiyaṁ tumaē, tahā vi kulabaiṇō । sīsau imaṁ sarūvaṁ avaṇṇavāō'ṇṇahā hōhī' ॥ 43 ॥ 1776 ॥
1. °vaṇaṁ pā0 vinā ।। 2. payattō tru0 kā0 ॥
10
<pb n="199"/>

tō kulavaiṇō kahiyaṁ tāvasasahiyassa tēṇa tō' kahiyaṁ । 'kiṁ kīrau ? ēva ṭhiē jaṁ saṁjāyaṁ tayaṁ jāyaṁ ॥ 44 ॥ 1777॥
tō tāvasījaṇēṇaṁ pālijaṁtī kamēṇa ya pasūyā । pasaraṁtapahāpayaraṁ puttaṁ surakumarasāricchaṁ ॥45॥1778॥
aṇuciyaāhārāō saṁjāō tīē dāruṇō rōgō । ōsahapāṇāīyaṁ kiriyaṁ jā tāvasīvaggō ॥ 46 ॥ 1779 ।।
kuṇai taō kammavasā ahiyayaraṁ cēva vaḍḍhaē rōgō । taṁ pēcchiūṇa sahasā uvvēvaṁ kuṇai tavasiyaṇō ॥ 47 ॥ 1780 ॥
" kaha kāhāmō ēvaṁ bālaṁ " ciṁtāurāṇa savvāṇa । bhaviyabvayāvasēṇaṁ harisapurāō tahiṁ pattō ॥ 48 ॥ 1781 ॥
nāmēṇa dēvadharō sahiō bhajāē dēvasēṇāē । ahiṇavapasūiyāē ujjēṇipurīē vatthavvō ॥49॥ 1782 |
sō tāvasāṇa bhattō jā pavisai āsamammi namaṇatthaṁ । tā tavasiyaṇaṁ pēcchai ciṁtā bharasāyaranimaggaṁ ॥ 50 ॥ 1783 ॥
vaṁdittu kulavaī tō pucchai ciṁtāi kāraṇaṁ sēṭṭhī । sō vi kahiūṇa savvaṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ॥51॥1784॥
'bhō ! bhō tāvasabhattaya ! dinnaṁ amhēhi gēṇhimaṁ bālaṁ । jēṇa'vagacchai ciṁtā' 'taha tti' paḍivajjaē sō vi ॥52॥ 1785॥
tō kulavaiṇā kumarō samappiō harisanibbharamaṇēṇa । 'gurudinnaō' tti kāuṁ tēṇā'vi paḍicchiō sammaṁ ॥ 53 ॥ 1786 ॥
dēvī vi jāyatōsā cittasamāhīē pāviyā maraṇaṁ । sēṭṭhī vi haṭutuṭṭhō gaṁtuṁ niyayammi āvāsē || 54 ॥ 1787॥
1. tāṁ bhaṇiyaṁ pā0 vinā ॥ 2. 'tāē jē0 kā0 ॥। 3. amhēhiṁ gihimaṁ truo ||
10
<pb n="200"/>

niyaparivāraṁ savvaṁ kāūṇaṁ savahasāviyaṁ bhaṇai । 'ujjēṇiṁ pattēhiṁ vattavyaṁ juyalayaṁ jāyaṁ' ॥55॥ 1788 ॥
' ēvaṁ ' ti pariyaṇēṇaṁ paḍivannē jāi niyayagēhammi । baddhāvaṇāi savvaṁ karēi hallamphalō inbhō ॥ 56 ॥ 1789॥
kumarassa amaradattōtti nāma vihiyaṁ kumāriyāē vi । surasuṁdari tti nāmaṁ kāūṇaṁ ṇivbuō jāō ॥57॥1790॥
vaḍḍhai ya amaradattō kīlaṁtō bahuvihāhi kīlāhiṁ । jāō ya tassa mittō mittāṇaṁdō tti nāmēṇaṁ ॥ 58 ॥ 1791॥
tatthēva ya vatthavvassa varasuō sāyarassa sēṭṭhissa । mittasirīnāmāē bhajāē kucchisaṁbhūō ॥ 59 ॥ 1792 ॥
tāṇaṁ ca tahiṁ mēttī aīva sahavaḍriḍhayāṇa tō jāyā । kiṁ bahuṇā ? samacittā sahaṁti na parōpparaviōgaṁ ॥60॥1793 ॥
aha annayā kayāī saṁpattō tattha pāusō kālō । alikajjalakālēhiṁ jalaēhiṁ nahaṁ samāuliyaṁ ॥ 61 ॥ 1794॥
vitthariō ghaṇasō viyārayaṁtō vya virahiṇīhiyayaṁ । tajjīyarddhavijū kayaṁtajīha vva vipphurai ||62|| 1795 ॥
muyai kayaṁtō vva ghaṇō dhārāniyaraṁ paryaḍakōyaṁḍō । virahiyaṇamāraṇatthaṁ sutikkhasarapasaraniyaraṁ va ॥ 63 ॥ 1796॥
bittharai daddararavō savvattō virahivajjhapaḍahō vva । tammaraṇē rōyaṁti va disāō jalabiṁdu aṁhiṁ ॥ 64 ॥1797॥
dīsai navahariyaṁ kurasamōtthayā iṁdagōvayasaṇāhā । bahurayaṇa jaḍiyamaragaya kuṭṭimasarisā vasumaīvi ||65 || 1798 ॥
ēyārisambhikālē kumarā tē dō vi sippaṇaitīrē । vaḍapāyava āsannē daṁḍāvēḍīhiṁ kīlaṁti ॥ 66 ॥ 1799॥
1. juvalayaṁ tru0 kā0 ॥। 2. navaruhiyaṁ ° kā0 ॥
10
